# Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Pass.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Pass.png) | Pass: Cold Rock Pass ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cold+Rock+Pass)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 8 |
| Occupants | |
| [Frost Troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ColdRockPassExterior01 (South Cold Rock Pass), ColdRockPassExterior02 (North Cold Rock Pass), ColdRockPass01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") (see [notes](#Notes)) | |
| Location | |
| South-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") North of [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 2 |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 2 |
| # of [Quicksilver](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") | 1 |

Cold Rock Pass

**Cold Rock Pass** is a small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through a mountain south-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll").

Although the interior of the ruin is named "Cold Rock Pass", the map markers for the two entrances are named "North Cold Rock Pass" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Cold+Rock+Pass&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "South Cold Rock Pass" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Cold+Rock+Pass&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The northern entrance is south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), and the southern entrance is northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior: North Cold Rock Pass

North Cold Rock Pass

The northern entrance is found by following the path southwest of Morthal toward [Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak"); when you pass a banner attached to a post on your left, the entrance is on the next switchback to the left. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is along the path near the entrance, and several [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes grow in the vicinity.

### Exterior: South Cold Rock Pass

South Cold Rock Pass

The southern entrance is found by ascending the stone stairs leading north to the left of the entrance of [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast"). A dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") is next to the entrance. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is down the hill to the entrance.

### Cold Rock Pass

Upon entering via the nothern entrance, you enter a natural cave heading down and to the west. Ahead is a wooden crate near a lootable skeleton and a sack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). To the south, to the left of an earthen ramp leading up is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). At the top of the ramp the cave opens up in front of you, with a couple rock pillars supporting the ceiling and a frozen pond of water being fed by a small waterfall. Southwest of the waterfall on a higher ledge is a frost troll. The ramp leading up to it is along the northwest wall of the cave.

The ledge has a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") on the southwest wall of the cave. Among the bones and blood splatters on the ground are some [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") or [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and a dead skeever or two. There may be the body of a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") by the edge, although this may have fallen off and be lying on the ice below. Near the frost troll is a dead [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") and an open chest holding a set of random armor, a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), and two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the south, below the ledge is a large shallow pond that has mostly frozen over, with the path through the cave beside it. Against the east wall, opposite the waterfall is a food barrel next to an unlocked chest. At the southern end of the pond is a second corundum ore vein, with a ramp up to its left leading past a cart containing a food barrel, a second barrel beside it, and a second lootable skeleton, ending at the southern entrance.

## Notes

- Although the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* places this location in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), the game data states it is in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. The pass has been set to be part of Hjaalmarch instead.
  - Technically, the pass itself is a transition between the two holds, with its southern entrance in Whiterun Hold and its northern entrance in Hjaalmarch, so either could be said to be applicable.
- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces all [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes outside North Cold Rock Pass with the snow-covered version of the same plant.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Maps

- 

  Cold Rock Pass

## Gallery

- 

  Skeleton and bone wolves near the southern entrance

# Skyrim:Coldcinder Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Coldcinder Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Coldcinder+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 20 |
| Occupants | |
| [Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), [Netches](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch"), [Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRBulwarkCave | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") North-northwest of [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Heart Stone Deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") | 3 |

Coldcinder Cave

**Coldcinder Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") and [netches](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch"). It contains only one zone, *[Coldcinder Cave](#Walkthrough)*.

There are two entrances to the cave, with the exterior entrance through a trapdoor atop the cliff just southeast of Raven Rock and another entrance via a door in the [Bulwark Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark_Jail "Skyrim:The Bulwark Jail"). The trapdoor entrance does not have a map marker, but can be found by climbing to the highest columnar basalt rock formation south of the [Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark") and north of [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow"); the trapdoor is just below the southern edge of this formation. The cave also allows for a cheap and easy escape from the jail; open the novice-locked grate in the jail cell and drop into the tunnel, follow the passage north to the ceiling grate with the prisoner's belongings chest in easy reach and drop through another unlocked grate in the floor, then continue down the narrow tunnel to enter the cave through the unlocked iron door to the east.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The entrance from the Bulwark Jail

The trapdoor entrance

There are several lootable skeletons scattered throughout the cave, with many [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster"), [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants, and [trama roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") found inside.

Through the entrance door from the jail is a wide flight of stairs leading down to the east. On the left is a collapsed ceiling spike trap near the bottom of the stairs, while at the end of the room are more stairs descending to a partially flooded tunnel, with the walls made of fractured rock. As you continue along, beware a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in the tunnel. The tunnel gradually bears to the south before opening into a large cavern with a small central island and waterfalls cascading down the walls. There is also a family of netches here; they can be easily dispatched at range with either magic or a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") from inside the tunnel, where they can't reach you. Once the netches are dealt with, several [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") are found around the central island and walls. The tunnel continues to the south before turning to the southwest and climbing an earthen ramp. From the top of the ramp, a series of bridges link several raised platforms crossing another partially flooded cavern to some dry land to the east-southeast, where there is a ladder that exits the cave via the trapdoor entrance above the Bulwark.

Coldcinder Cave interior

From the dry land, it is possible to explore the partially flooded area of this second cavern. There are a few more pearl oysters in this area, and a tunnel heading southwest which eventually opens into a third cavern that rises to the southwest. Following the northwest wall to the end leads to a series of flights of stairs that climb the bank. At the top is a plateau with a leveled ash spawn that will rise from the ground on the left, with rubble and debris scattered all around. There are a few minor items in this area, including two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") along the northwest wall near a skeleton, and a [honed draugr war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Draugr_War_Axe "Skyrim:Honed Draugr War Axe") opposite along the southeast wall near another skeleton. Near the entrance to the third cavern and nearly buried in ash are two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") and a set of shelves holding a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Ahead to the southwest are more stairs leading up to another area at the rear of the cavern. At the top is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") deposits, one each to either side of the chest against the rear wall. In front of these deposits, two more leveled ash spawn rise from the ground.

From the chest, head north to the far wall to a third heart stone deposit; along the wall to the right of the deposit is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") on a ledge above. Behind the urn, at the very back of the ledge is a skeleton with an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet"), a [honed ancient Nord sword of cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Ancient_Nord_Sword_of_Cold "Skyrim:Honed Ancient Nord Sword of Cold"), and a [silver and moonstone circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_and_Moonstone_Circlet "Skyrim:Silver and Moonstone Circlet"). Returning to the chest and facing east-northeast, there is a second chest on a raised platform around a stone pillar, which can be reached either from the edge at the top of the highest level using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") or by clever jumping and climbing. The chest is novice-locked, and has an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") beside it.

Coldhearted Gravedigger

The **Coldhearted Gravedigger** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who may appear in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") during the quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). She is one of ten possible targets.

The Gravedigger wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots") and a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") in combat.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

## Quest-Related Events

If spoken to she will say:

:   *"I'm dying for a rest. I swear, I could lie down right now, and just sleep forever."*

Colette Marence

**Colette Marence** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [monk](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerRestorationExpert "Skyrim:TrainerRestorationExpert") and an instructor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). She is the expert [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), able to train you to level 75, and sells several [Restoration spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells").

She wears [master robes of restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Robes_of_Restoration "Skyrim:Master Robes of Restoration") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000d3e09 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She knows a number of spells, namely [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh"), [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"), [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks"), [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward"), and [Turn Lesser Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Lesser_Undead "Skyrim:Turn Lesser Undead").

Colette can be found in her room on the second floor of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"), especially during the later hours of the night. During the day, she can also sometimes be found sitting in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), especially in the morning.

## Related Quests

- **[Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell")**: Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.
- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
- **[Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment")**: Deal with the aftermath of the Eye's power surge.
- **[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")**: Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

### Good Intentions

You can ask Colette about the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"):

:   **Have you ever heard of the Augur of Dunlain?**
:   *"The Augur? Tragic story, really. At least, the way I heard it. But that was a long time ago. It was some experiment gone horribly wrong. Ghastly results, I was told. And his ghost still roams the halls, they say. Of course, on further reflection, that may have simply been an attempt to scare me. Hmm. Perhaps I'll ask Tolfdir what really happened. I understand he was here at the time."*

### Containment

Colette will be standing with other members of the College, and will say:

:   *"This can't be happening!"*

### The Staff of Magnus

While leaving the Hall of the Elements for the [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"), Colette will say to you:

:   *"You'll defeat Ancano, won't you?"*
:   *"What are we going to do? How do we save the College?"*

### The Black Star

During the quest [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star"), you can ask Colette if she knows of [an Elven mage in the college that studies stars.](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar")

:   **Is there an elven mage here that studies stars?**
:   *"Why would anyone bother to study stars? Well, unless you're talking about that artifact that got all those... dimwits thrown out."*

:   :   **What is it? What happened?**
    :   *"Oh, no, I'm not falling for that one again. Next thing I know, I'm getting yelled at for saying something inappropriate. If you're so curious, talk to Nelacar, in the Frozen Hearth. He can tell you the whole sad story."*

:   :   **Would you believe I was given a vision?**
    :   *"Oh no, I'm not talking about that. I'm not being blamed for saying something out of place. Again. If you want to know, ask Nelacar. He's staying at the Frozen Hearth. Knows the whole sad story."*

### Restoration Ritual Spell

Upon reaching level 90 in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), and after completing the quest [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), you can ask Colette if there is anything more to be learned within Restoration:

:   **What else is there to be learned about Restoration Magic?**
:   *"Look at you. Such a devoted student of Restoration. It's comforting to see that not everyone has dismissed it as entirely as most members of the College. Truly comforting. It looks like you're ready to speak with the Augur."*

:   :   **What does the Augur have to do with this?**
    :   *"Oh, didn't you know?"*

:   :   **I thought you were the authority on this subject.**
    :   *"Oh, goodness no. There are those far more skilled than I."*

In either case, she will continue, saying:

:   *"The Augur was a brilliant mage. Truly inspired. Mastered spells others could barely comprehend. He was especially gifted when it came to Restoration. He's... Well, he's very particular about who shares the knowledge. So you'll need his approval first. Go on, go talk to him. I'm sure he's been paying attention, and will be expecting you."*

## Dialogue

She is extremely paranoid about being ridiculed by her peers at the college due to her study in Restoration magic. Upon first meeting her, she will appear highly agitated and demand:

:   *"You consider Restoration a valid school of magic, worthy of study, don't you? Don't you?"*

:   :   **Of course it's valid.**
    :   *"Good, good. Not that I require validation, of course. There are just some - and I shan't name names - who would disagree. It can make life difficult when one's colleagues fail to recognize the research one engages in."*

:   :   **Not really.**
    :   *"I... I see. Well, I'm glad we've established this early, rather than me hearing about it years or decades later when the whispers behind my back are loud enough."*

Either way it will lead to:

:   **So you're treated badly because of your work?**
:   *"Well... No. Not really. Not directly, I mean. But I know things are said behind my back. Conversations cease when I enter rooms. I'm quite aware of what's going on here, and I will not stand for it!"*
:   **I don't understand.**
:   *"It's quite simple really. There are some who shall not be dignified by being named, who have implied that it is not. That is to say, it's been suggested that resources used for my study of Restoration could be put to better use. Any other use, in fact. It's not just healing cuts and bruises, you know. The undead are a very real, very dangerous threat and Restoration magics can keep them at bay. Not to mention the benefit of wards! How can they continually overlook wards! It's baffling!"*

When beginning or ending a conversation with Colette, she can say:

:   *"Why are my research materials constantly disappearing?"*
:   *"Once again, I have found very insulting notes left in my personal effects. Simply barbaric."*
:   *"Just because I don't fit in here is no reason for others to ridicule me behind my back."*
:   *"Restoration is a perfectly valid school of magic, and don't let anyone tell you otherwise!"*

If you ask her to train you in Restoration magic, she will say:

:   *"I'll gladly share my knowledge with you."*

### Restoration Magic Lecture

Colette giving a lecture

Like many other members of the College, Colette will give lectures in the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"), hers being on Restoration magic. The lecture comes off as more of a scolding diatribe, however, about how outrageous it is that the school of Restoration is so disrespected at the college:

:   *"I would just like to remind everyone, once again, that Restoration is indeed a valid school of magic. It is absolutely worthy of research, despite many of the notes I've had left in my bed. And my desk. And on occasion, my meals. Anyone suggesting that Restoration is better left to the priests of the Temples, I think, is forgetting a few things. Firstly, the ability to repel the undead cannot be ignored. Skyrim is well known to be full of these... Draugr, ancient Nord warriors who cannot find peace. I submit that everyone in this College has, at one time or another, relied on one of the Restoration spells that can keep them at bay. Secondly, how can anyone forget wards? They have become essential to any mage working in dangerous situations. They are counted upon every bit as much as Candlelight, or Invisibility. But more importantly, wards have saved lives. This is a simple fact. Every mage in this College regularly uses wards for practice, so as to avoid physical harm. I truly hope that these points actually sink in, and that more care and thought is given to this subject in the future. Thank you."*

## Conversations

While inside the Arcanaeum, she may have conversations with other College members, such as [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"):

:   **Colette:** *"Ah, my dearest Urag! How are you today, my green-skinned friend?"*
:   **Urag:** *"Did you need something, Colette?"*
:   **Colette:** *"I only wish to escape the constant glaring of my 'colleagues' and discover an opportunity for repose. Your Arcanaeum is so lovely and quiet..."*
:   **Urag:** *"I... see."*
:   **Colette:** *"Don't fret, my fanged acquaintance. I shan't trouble you a bit."*

:   **Urag:** *"Was there something specific you needed?"*
:   **Colette:** *"I'm positive whatever I require will be revealed to me on its own, in due time."*
:   **Urag:** *"So, you don't need anything then."*
:   **Colette:** *"Oh, my dear Urag. You're trying so hard to help. I do hope you're not disappointed."*
:   **Urag:** *"'Disappointed' is not the word I would choose, Colette. Excuse me."*

She also attempts to make conversation with [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren"), who reacts in a similarly terse and dismissive manner:

:   **Colette:** *"How are you, Drevis?"*
:   **Drevis:** *"Ugh. What do you want?"*
:   **Colette:** *"Why should I want anything? Why can't I simply be sociable with my colleagues?"*
:   **Drevis:** *"I'm busy right now, Colette."*
:   **Colette:** *"Well, then. Fine. Have a nice day."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Colette's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Complete set of Novice [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") |  |
| 1 | Complete set of Apprentice [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") |  |
| 1 | Complete set of Adept [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") | Only if PC's skill level is ≥ 40 |
| 1 | Complete set of Expert [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") | Only if PC's skill level is ≥ 65 |
| 5 | Leveled Mages Hood (enchanted) |  |
| 5 | Leveled Mages Robes (enchanted) |  |
| 10 | Leveled Restoration Robes |  |
| ~9 | Leveled [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") | Max 12 (12@75%) |
| ~15 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 20 (20@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| 1 | [Mage Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage_Hood "Skyrim:Mage Hood") |  |

## Notes

- It seems that when Colette is trying to get past the protective ward in [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") she can actually run off the bridge if you don't get it down fast enough. She will lose her path if this happens and remain where she lands until found. Using Detect Life under the bridge of the college should allow you to find her if this is the case. By pushing her far enough towards the town (not the college), she will eventually pick up the path back to normal life.
- Colette Marence also appears in the [Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim") card expansion for *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, as the card [Restoration Tutor](/wiki/Legends:Restoration_Tutor "Legends:Restoration Tutor"), although her race does not match.
- When you speak to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") for the first time, she will comment on Colette, saying *"And finally, there's Colette. She may be... difficult to get along with, she's very knowledgeable when it comes to Restoration magic."*
- Colette's insecurity about the perceived validity of Restoration as a school of magic, particularly the idea that it would be "better left to the priests of the Temples", may be a reference to [Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind") where Restoration (along with Conjuration) are strangely absent from the list of favored skills that can be used to advance in rank in the [Mages Guild](/wiki/Morrowind:Mages_Guild "Morrowind:Mages Guild") despite being a form of magic, but which can be found in the skill lists for the [Imperial Cult](/wiki/Morrowind:Imperial_Cult "Morrowind:Imperial Cult") and [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Morrowind:Tribunal_Temple "Morrowind:Tribunal Temple") factions.

## Bugs

- Even after you finish the Restoration Ritual Spell quest, Colette still may not sell the Guardian Circle spell.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:College Objective Quest

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Visit the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Innkeepers and Spell Merchants |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | MG01Pointer |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") | | |

Travel to the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") in hope of gaining entry

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Hear or ask about the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
2. Travel to [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and approach the College.

## Detailed Walkthrough

During conversations with certain NPCs, namely innkeepers and spell merchants, you may be given the option to ask them about magic training. You will usually be directed to either the local city's court mage or the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") itself. Asking about the college directly will result in a new map marker and also brings up a [miscellaneous](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Quests") quest to visit the College of Winterhold.

### Arriving At The College

After arriving in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), you can see the college and the bridge leading to it. When attempting to cross the bridge, [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), a college mage guarding the bridge from unwanted visitors, will stop you and initiate the first college-related quest, [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons").

## Bugs

- This quest may be shown as incomplete if you successfully persuade [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), the Gatekeeper.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Use the console command `setstage MG01Pointer 200` to complete it.
- The quest may also show as incomplete (and will point you to Nirya) if you tell Faralda that you are Dragonborn and show her your "shout".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG01Pointer stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG01Pointer`.

# Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-College_of_Winterhold.png) | Guild Hall: College of Winterhold ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=College+of+Winterhold)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:College_of_Winterhold "Lore:College of Winterhold")) | | |
| # of Zones | 7 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WinterholdCollegeArcanaeum WinterholdCollegeArchMageQuarters WinterholdCollegeHallofAttainment WinterholdCollegeHallofCountenance WinterholdCollegeHalloftheElements WinterholdCollegeMidden01  WinterholdCollegeMidden02 | |
| Location | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 4 |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 2 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 2 |

Entrance to the College

The **College of Winterhold** is a school of the arcane arts.

Dusk view overlooking Winterhold

The College of Winterhold

The College is located in the snowy northern city of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), in the [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") of the same name, overlooking the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). It functions much like the [Mages Guild](/wiki/Lore:Mages_Guild "Lore:Mages Guild") in [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") or [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), but is a completely independent organization from [Tamriel's](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") other mage training centers. The College has struggled to maintain its prominence in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") in recent years for a number of different reasons. The Nords, already skeptical of magic, have become increasingly suspicious of the College because it came out unscathed during the [Great Collapse](/wiki/Lore:Great_Collapse "Lore:Great Collapse") that largely destroyed Winterhold. Additionally, while the College maintains standards for what kind of activities are allowed on campus, in contrast to the [Mages Guild](/wiki/Oblivion:Mages_Guild "Oblivion:Mages Guild"), it regards [Necromancy](/wiki/Lore:Necromancy "Lore:Necromancy") as a viable arcane practice.

The College is a very secure and selective school, only allowing entry to those they deem worthy. An [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") sorcerer named [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") guards the entrance from the main part of Winterhold to the College and warns you that you will likely not be allowed entry. Despite this warning you will never be refused entry after completing the minor [task](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") she sets. The College itself, a large fortress-like structure, is located atop an apparently precarious rock formation, in the shape of an upside-down pyramid. It is connected to the city of Winterhold by a long stone bridge with several focal points along its length. Portions of the bridge have crumbled away into the sea below leaving a section that is easy to fall from. The College is sealed by a large gate with the top wrought into the shape of the College symbol as depicted on their banners. There is an identical seal set into the ground at the start of the bridge.

## Layout

The College consists of three structures separated by a central courtyard featuring a large statue of a mage, and connected by walkways at ground level and along the top of the walls that surround the complex. The main building contains a library, called the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"), which is used for all kinds of magical practice and serves as a lecture hall, and the [Arch-Mage's quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters"), the residence of the head of the College. Accommodations for students and faculty members are provided in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") and the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"), respectively. Beneath the College complex lies [the Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden"), an underground remnant of the College's past.

Entry is gained into the College by telling Faralda what you seek to learn and then casting a spell of her choice. If you are on the quest [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge"), you can choose to demonstrate a [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") instead. Alternatively, she can be persuaded if your speech skill is high enough. After you prove your worthiness, she will guide you into the College and refer you to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") to begin your apprenticeship.

Note that Faralda does not always demand the same spell. She will randomly ask you to cast one of the following spells: [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight"), [Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Healing Hands"), or [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"). If you do not already know the spell she demands, she will offer to sell it to you for 30 gold. Saving before talking to her is recommended in case you do not have the magicka to cast the required spell, allowing you to reload until she chooses a spell that you can cast.

# No longer a resident after completing [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") quest.
† No longer a resident after completing [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") quest.
\* Becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") only after completing the [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") quest.
‡ No longer a resident after completing [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") quest.
% No longer a resident after initiating the [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment") quest.

## Magical Training and Learning Spells

The College of Winterhold is staffed by teachers who also serve as spell vendors for the skill they specialize in. While they are willing to train you and buy and sell various items, they will only sell you spell tomes based on your corresponding skill level. For example, if you are interested in buying the Invisibility spell book, you will need to have an Illusion skill level above 65.

## Lectures

After [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons"), mages at the College hold various lectures. Although the lecture is chosen each day between noon and 1pm, due to participant travel time most begin after 2pm. If there is any danger at the College (such as a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack), then a lecture will not occur for the next 24 hours. The lectures all take place within the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements").

### Colette Marence : Restoration Magic

*"I would just like to remind everyone, once again, that Restoration is indeed a valid school of magic. It is absolutely worthy of research, despite many of the notes I've had left in my bed. And my desk. And on occasion, my meals. Anyone suggesting that Restoration is better left to the priests of the Temples, I think, is forgetting a few things. Firstly, the ability to repel the undead cannot be ignored. Skyrim is well known to be full of these... [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), ancient Nord warriors who cannot find peace. I submit that everyone in this College has, at one time or another, relied on one of the Restoration spells that can keep them at bay. Secondly, how can anyone forget wards? They have become essential to any mage working in dangerous situations. They are counted upon every bit as much as [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight"), or [Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)"). But more importantly, wards have saved lives. This is a simple fact. Every mage in this College regularly uses wards for practice, so as to avoid physical harm. I truly hope that these points actually sink in, and that more care and thought is given to this subject in the future. Thank you."*

### Drevis Neloren : Doomstones

*"The existence of so-called "Doomstones" throughout Skyrim has been repeatedly verified. The meaning of these stones has not. The prevailing opinion of Skyrim natives is that the stones are indeed magical in nature. While there is no direct evidence of this, it does seem likely. References to similar stones appear in lore throughout the various Tamrielic cultures. None, however, exactly match the markings or distribution of Skyrim's stones. At present, there is no confirmation of any of the various theories surrounding the nature of these stones. Their relative positions do not indicate that any individual stone is part of a larger, unobserved pattern. Also, their placement throughout Skyrim does not correspond to any known magical phenomenon. The age of the stones themselves has yet to be officially determined. It has been widely assumed that they were placed during the Merethic Era. Writings from that period, including those of [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor") himself, do not mention the stones and thus this idea cannot be verified. Nonetheless, many are drawn to these stones based on the local stories describing them as a source of significant power. The College will continue to research these intriguing objects, and of course any findings will be relayed with all possible haste."*

### Faralda : External Pressures

*"It is no secret that both the [Synod](/wiki/Lore:Synod "Lore:Synod") and the [College of Whispers](/wiki/Lore:College_of_Whispers "Lore:College of Whispers") have recently made inquiries as to the status of our College here in Winterhold. At this time, there is no indication that either group is aware of the other's correspondence. The College of Winterhold has thus far declined requests for direct meetings. This has been at the specific request of [Arch-Mage Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"). Aren believed that although the initial communications were innocent enough, they were sent with a particular motive in mind. The Synod's harsh rules and draconian structure are maintained only by suppressing any opposition to their Council's policies. It is entirely possible that they look to our College here in Winterhold in order to find supporters for their organization. Likewise, the College of Whispers has long been driven by its desire to directly oppose the Synod. They focus on research banned by the Synod, such as Conjuration and Necromancy. The College of Whispers hopes to learn that our College also supports these avenues of research. Thus they may claim that the Synod is indeed a political minority in the Empire and should be treated as such. Our actual position and policies are irrelevant. No matter the facts of the response, it will certainly be twisted to suit the whims of either group. Indeed, it has been jokingly suggested that we send the exact same response to both, which each will warp into support for their side. At present, these two groups do little beyond attempting to gain the attention and favor of the Emperor. They appear to have little interest in real study and research for the sake of gaining knowledge. Arch-Mage Aren believes that their conflict poses a significant threat to the autonomy of our College, and I concur. Falling in with either would threaten to draw much unwanted attention to our College. If either group goes through less official channels and attempt*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *to contact you directly, please refer them to the College's Master Wizard. Say as little as possible so as to avoid compromising our neutral position."*

### Phinis Gestor : College Policy

*"At this time, I would like to make a few statements regarding policy here at the College. Any information as to the whereabouts of the previous group of Apprentices would be greatly appreciated. As of yet, there has been no sign of them. [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") remains off-limits at this time; while the initial outbreak has been cleaned up, the area is still considered hazardous. No more experiments are to be carried out there, and mages are advised that you enter the Midden at your own risk. Once again, I must ask that everyone please clean up any materials used in the common areas. We've had yet another sprained ankle due to [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") being left on the floor. Let's please try and keep injuries to a minimum."*

### Phinis Gestor: College Policy

*"At this time, I would like to make a few statements regarding policy here at the College. Please refrain from practicing Conjuration spells in view of the town of Winterhold. Atronachs have a tendency to frighten the locals. Undead.... well, I don't even think it needs to be said. While [Drevis](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") appreciates the spellcasting skill that went into somehow cramming several hundred apples into his pillow... He would ask that it please not happen again. He has suggested that, should he find out who is responsible, he is well versed in making things disappear permanently."*

### Phinis Gestor: College Policy

*"At this time, I would like to make a few statements regarding policy here at the College. [Urag](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") has asked me to remind everyone to please return materials borrowed from [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") in the same condition as you received them. If this is impossible due to misuse or accident, Urag recommends finding a replacement copy to deliver to the Arcanaeum. Failure to do so will result in paying, in Urag's words, "a blood price." I did not ask him to elaborate on that point. There have been unconfirmed reports that someone has been sneaking into the town of Winterhold while invisible, and causing... issues. This goes quite against College policy, and the party responsible is advised to cease these actions at once."*

### Phinis Gestor: Policy on the Eye

*"Projects are underway to discern the origin and nature of the College's recent find in Saarthal. Any and all theories are currently being considered. Those with ideas should please speak with [Mirabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine"). At this time, there is no indication that, as has been rumored, the object is in fact a physical part of Magnus, the god of magic. It has been suggested that the object is a gateway to the realm of [Aetherius](/wiki/Lore:Aetherius "Lore:Aetherius"), but nothing has proven that idea one way or the other. It has been proposed that the object is in fact the entirety of Aurbis in one physical space. This would of course mean that [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"), indeed all of Mundus, is actually contained within the sphere. It further suggests that we are somehow then outside our own existence while looking in at it. While the idea seems dubious at best, it has not, at present, been entirely ruled out."*

### Urag gro-Shub : Shalidor's Works

Statue to Shalidor

*"As many know, there is an ongoing effort to research the work of the Archmagus Shalidor. He is most remembered for his great maze of [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"), said to hold "Glamoril", or the secret of life. While stories have persisted since the First Era, none have ever confirmed the existence of this "Glamoril" or its purpose or function. The College has developed some theories, however. We know that Shalidor had an understanding of magic that surpassed almost any of either his age or ours. The few works of his that have been recovered suggest that he had an understanding of magic and the world that few have ever achieved. What is interesting is that it appears he was also incredibly prolific, writing on a diverse array of subjects. An array so great, in fact, that it remains a source of curiosity. What, then, of this Glamoril? It means "secret of life" in elvish. Could this be an explanation for Shalidor's works? Is it possible that it somehow contributed to his work? Perhaps allowed him to life*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *multiple lifetimes in a short span of time? Increased his intelligence and knowledge in ways unfathomable to us? We may never know for certain. The College is always searching for more of Shalidor's writings in an attempt to understand both our knowledge of the man, and of magic in general."*

#### Primary Quests

- **[First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons")**: Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
- **[Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal")**: Uncover the mysteries beneath this ancient ruin.
- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").
- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
- **[Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen")**: Learn the location of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").
- **[Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment")**: Deal with the aftermath of the Eye's power surge.
- **[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")**: Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").
- **[The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus")**: Reclaim the College and contain the Eye.

#### Side Quests

- **[Aftershock](/wiki/Skyrim:Aftershock "Skyrim:Aftershock")**: Put an end to the rupture caused by the Eye of Magnus. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Brelyna's Practice](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna%27s_Practice "Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice")**: Help [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") by allowing her to practice her spells on you.
- **[J'zargo's Experiment](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Experiment "Skyrim:J'zargo's Experiment")**: Help [a student](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") test out a fiery new spell.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights")**: Discover the writings of Shalidor and benefit from his wisdom. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Master Skill Quests

- **[Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell")**: Acquire [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang") and use it to get [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell")**: Find a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") by summoning a daedra and learn more about [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration").
- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.
- **[Illusion Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell")**: Find some books about [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") magic to further your Illusion skills.
- **[Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell")**: Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Enchanting Pick-Up](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Pick-Up "Skyrim:Enchanting Pick-Up")**: [Sergius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") wants you to pick up an item from a client for enchanting. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!")**: Fetch a book for [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Forgotten Names](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Names "Skyrim:Forgotten Names")**: Summon the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") pirate, [Velehk Sain](/wiki/Skyrim:Velehk_Sain "Skyrim:Velehk Sain"). (non-journal)
- **[Forgotten Vale Books Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Bring the Ancient Falmer Tome to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
- **[Out of Balance](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance")**: Purify the focus points for magical energy around the College of Winterhold.
- **[Rejoining the College](/wiki/Skyrim:Rejoining_the_College "Skyrim:Rejoining the College")**: Make amends for breaking the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") rules.
- **[Restocking Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Restocking_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Restocking Soul Gems")**: Help [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") to fill his stock with [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").
- **[Tolfdir the Absent-Minded](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir_the_Absent-Minded "Skyrim:Tolfdir the Absent-Minded")**: Help [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") find his missing [alembic](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir%27s_Alembic "Skyrim:Tolfdir's Alembic").

#### Creation Club

- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").
- **[Creature of Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Creature_of_Legend "Skyrim:Creature of Legend")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Track down and tame the last living [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn").
- **[Swift as an Arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Swift_as_an_Arrow "Skyrim:Swift as an Arrow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack"): Learn how to craft and use [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow").

#### Incomplete Quests

- **[Filling Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Filling_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Filling Soul Gems")**: Fill a [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Soul Gem") for [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus"). ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))
- **[Research Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Research_Thief "Skyrim:Research Thief")**: Steal [Faralda's notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Faralda's Notes") for [Nirya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirya "Skyrim:Nirya"). ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))
- **[Rogue Wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue_Wizard "Skyrim:Rogue Wizard")**: Deal with a rogue wizard for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"). ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))
- **[The Missing Apprentices](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Missing_Apprentices "Skyrim:The Missing Apprentices")**: Discover the fate of [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor")'s missing apprentices. ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))

## Notes

- There are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") near the College. Instead of taking the ramp to the gate, walk around to its right. One vein is a short distance ahead, while the other is further up to the northwest.
- For those unable or unwilling to undergo the initiation test given by Faralda, the College can be indirectly accessed through the cave opening of the Midden. This gives non-initiates access to most of the College's [benefits](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Benefits "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
- Be careful when fast-traveling to the College on horseback, as you will spawn on a narrow section of the bridge, making it easy to fall off and die if you are not careful.
- With the [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), your tamed [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn") will return here if you switch to a different mount.
- The College of Winterhold also [appears](/wiki/Legends:College_of_Winterhold "Legends:College of Winterhold") in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, in the *[Return to Clockwork City](/wiki/Legends:Return_to_Clockwork_City "Legends:Return to Clockwork City")* storyline.

## Bugs

- The stairways between the Hall of Elements, the Arcanaeum, and the Arch-Mage's Quarters act in strange ways. Entering from the ground floor, both the Arcanaeum and the Arch-Mage's Quarters seem to be on the floor above, in an arrangement that would have them both occupy the same physical space. There are stairs that lead between the two, however. This may be a bug in the links between cells, or an intentional extra-dimensional oddity of the College. This glitch also messes with an NPC's pathfinding abilities, forcing them to travel through the Arch-Mage's Quarters when they need to travel between the Arcanaeum and the Hall of the Elements.
- Dismissing Brelyna, Onmund, or J'zargo as followers after they've been married or recruited as Blades still plays dialogue saying they're returning here when this is not where they'll be going.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Although the lecture choice checks for a dead lecturer, they can die on their way, hanging the scene.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Arniel Gane attempts to travel all the way from Saarthal for the lecture during Under Saarthal (MG02).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- Unlike all other lecturers, Colette's takes place between 1pm and 2pm. But this doesn't leave enough time for most participants to arrive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Lectures could stop occurring due to frequent polling, intensive loops, and other errors in the scripting that eventually slow all scripts to a halt.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Coming of Age

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. |  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help a [daring adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") and [her companion](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja") retrieve their riches.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Salma](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") |
| Location(s): | [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow") |

| ID: | dunIronbindQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

Salma and Beem-Ja at the entrance to Ironbind Barrow

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Meet [Salma](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") and [Beem-Ja](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja") outside [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow") and speak with Salma.
2. Escort Salma and Beem-Ja through the ruins until a fight with [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik") begins.
3. Kill Beem-Ja and speak with Salma.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The quest begins as soon as you arrive at [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow") and witness an argument between [Beem-Ja](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja") and [Salma](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") about venturing into the ruins. Speak with Salma and she will decide there's enough treasure for everyone and enter the ruins. Unfortunately, she and Beem-Ja must not really believe that there's enough to go around, because once inside they incessantly charge headlong into rooms full of leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). Although they can't actually be killed by any of the mobs in the barrow, you can accidentally kill one or both of them as they may jump in front of you during the fights; frequent game saves are strongly advised in case they are killed.

Salma and Beem-Ja will rush ahead and make short work of the [spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") in the first passage whether you help or not. When you arrive in a large room with a double staircase leading up to an east-west landing with a locked gate heading north, loot the chest on the east side of the landing before pulling the handle in the alcove on the west end to open the gate.

Proceed north down the passage into a circular room with a floor grating, two leveled draugr, a chest on the west wall and some minor loot on and near the table. Salma and Beem-Ja will rush ahead. Take the exit in the northeast corner and follow the hall around and down to the west, where you will see a chest behind a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") in the alcove directly ahead. You can loot both the chest and the helm next to it without crossing the pressure plate.

Go north from there to find the two friends trying to kill two more leveled draugr at the end of a short eastward-heading bridge. There's some minor loot on the floor and on the table and shelves to the south, plus an adept-locked chest in the southwest corner of the platform beside the wooden partition.

Descend the log ramp southward from the end of the bridge and chase Salma and Beem-Ja through the gate and into the next room. Defeat the two draugr there, then collect the few potions around the room and follow your charges out to the east, into a wide passage with a helmet on a [pedestal](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") in front of a closed gate. Notice the ominous black holes in the floor around the pedestal, and stand back a bit to loot the helm so that the spear trap doesn't kill you as the gate opens. Alternatively, if you stand at the pedestal, turn around so your back is to it, and look at the ceiling, there is a chain you can pull to open the gate without triggering the trap. Follow the hall to the iron doors and save your game before opening them, for the boss fight against [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik"), at least one draugr or skeleton and possibly a [frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"), is next.

Fight Gathrik as you would any Draugr or Dragon Priest. His tactics will vary based on his abilities.

Beem-Ja is scripted to start walking away when you open the door to Gathrik's chamber, avoiding the final fight. He will wander around a safe distance until Gathrik is killed, at which point he will run back and reveal his true colors. To prevent this, you can body-block him until the approaching minions trigger his aggression, at which point he will become an asset like Salma. After Gathrik is defeated, a script restores Beej-Ja to full health when he betrays you.

As soon as you defeat Gathrik, Beem-Ja thanks you for your help and asks you to hold still while he kills you for a blood sacrifice that he needs to perform in order to help him absorb Gathrik's power. Apparently, he's a necromancer. Killing him as soon as the dialogue releases you is highly recommended. Beem-Ja may [reanimate](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate") Gathrik's body to fight for him.

After Beem-Ja has been defeated, Salma will express her disbelief at his treachery but adds that her father never trusted him to begin with. She says that she now wants to be alone and decides to leave the ruins on her own, explaining that she no longer wants the treasure. Among Beem-Ja's loot is a [letter from Salma's father](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Letter to Beem-Ja") threatening to expose whatever unspecified evil Beem-Ja did back in Black Marsh if he allows any harm to come to Salma.

The [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") is behind Gathrik's throne at the north end of the upper level, and a boss-level unlocked chest is just to the west of the word wall. The exit is on the eastern side of the lower level, activated by a pull chain on the wall just to the right of the gate. Climb up the spiral stairway and exit to *Ironbind Overlook*, then unbar the door in front of you and exit to find an unlocked chest.

Be sure to continue past the chest around to the left and up the hill to find an unusual Dwarven monument with three pillars guarded by two Ice Wraiths; see [unmarked places](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Ruins_and_Monuments "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") for full details.

## Notes

- The [Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe_of_Fiery_Souls "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls") can be found mounted behind Gathrik's throne. It's the only weapon in the game that can be disenchanted to learn the [Fiery Soul Trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Fiery_Soul_Trap "Skyrim:Fiery Soul Trap") effect.
- Beem-Ja is capable of reanimating Gathrik; if he succeeds, the battle may become much more difficult. However, if you are able to loot Gathrik before he is reanimated, he will be much easier to defeat the second time.
- Although helping Salma is a quest-like activity, it does not function as a regular quest, providing no quest updates or rewards.
- Warlord Gathrik is leveled based on your level when the quest starts, and he has a chance of spawning as a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") after you reach level 40.
- If you are quick enough to loot Gathrik before Beem-Ja resurrects him, you can use one of Gathrik's black soul gems to soul trap Beem-Ja. Salma can be trapped in the other as killing her is consequence free. She disappears from the game after the quest is complete anyway.
- At very low levels Beem-Ja will not have any offensive spells and will fight only using unarmed melee attacks.
- Beem-Ja has a chance of having an enchanted circlet in his inventory. If he does, he will equip it and will be unable to wear his hooded robes. This will make him appear to be naked.
- If Salma gets disarmed, she may equip the Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls. If this happens, it cannot be pickpocketed (at least not without the [Misdirection](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket#Misdirection "Skyrim:Pickpocket") perk); you will have to kill her to retrieve it. To avoid this, run quickly to the back of the throne as soon you enter the chamber, and take the battleaxe yourself.

## Bugs

- At a certain point in Ironbind Barrow, there is a gate that must be opened by a switch. When Beem-Ja arrives at this gate, he'll comment on how there must be a way through, but if you've already opened the gate when his dialogue triggers then he and Salma may just stand there.
  - Close and open the gate again so they notice you opened it.
- Salma and Beem-Ja are marked as Protected, not Essential, meaning that you can accidentally kill either of them during combat, at which point the other will start walking back to the entrance and return to their respective position at the campfire outside Ironbind Barrow.
  - Resurrecting the killed NPC using the console does not correct this, but will result in both NPCs returning to the campfire.
  - If Beem-Ja is killed and Salma returns to the campfire, she resumes her post-quest dialogue.
  - If Salma is killed, Beem-Ja simply stays where he is. He may become hostile toward you, but will return to normal if you successfully hide from him.
- Arriving in the area may not initiate the quest, nor will speaking to either adventurer afterward.
- Before opening the gate if you go back into the previous room and just past the short set of stairs turn to the left (would be the same side of the room as the chest is in, but back further) there is a corner in the rocks if you keep walking through it will turn light bluish and it drops you to a hall right before the chamber with the word wall.
- It appears to be possible for Salma to disappear or be lost during the quest. The quest will proceed correctly, and Beem-Ja will still attack upon reaching the Ironbind Barrow throne room.
- Salma and Beem-Ja may both disappear from the game upon entering Ironbind Barrow. Since neither of them have a permanent RefID, it will be impossible to complete the quest.
  -  It might help to find the RefIDs for both of them in the output of console command `sqv dunIronbindQST`, which should be listed as `REF 'Salma'` and `REF 'Beem-Ja'`.

## Quest Stages

| Coming of Age (dunIronbindQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 20, 30, 40, 45, 50, 60, 70, 79, 80, 81, 90, 100.

  Notes
- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunIronbindQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunIronbindQST`.

# Skyrim:Commander Caius

## Overview

| Commander Caius (RefID: 00038258) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | | |
| House | [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks "Skyrim:Guard Barracks") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |

"Skyrim:During sieges, staff and family hide."); [Guard Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Faction_(for_dialogue) "Skyrim:Guard Faction (for dialogue)"); [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"); [GuardFactionWhiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFactionWhiterun "Skyrim:GuardFactionWhiterun"); [Imperial Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Government "Skyrim:Imperial Government"); [JobGuardCaptainFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobGuardCaptainFaction "Skyrim:JobGuardCaptainFaction"); [Ruling Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruling_Government "Skyrim:Ruling Government"); [TownWhiterunFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction "Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction") | | |

Commander Caius

**Commander Caius** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier (class)") stationed in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). He is in charge of the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") patrolling the hold under Jarl [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater").

Caius wears a set of [Whiterun guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard's Armor") and a pair of [fur boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Boots "Skyrim:Fur Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") which can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality, and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Whiterun, his position is taken by [Sinmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinmir "Skyrim:Sinmir"). Caius will then move to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") together with Balgruuf, [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") and [Irileth](/wiki/Skyrim:Irileth "Skyrim:Irileth").

## Related Quests

- **[Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits")**: Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.

## Dialogue

As long as Whiterun is under control of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), he may greet you in a number of ways. He may simply introduce himself:

:   *"I'm the commander of the guard here in Whiterun."*
:   *"My boys'll keep you safe. Don't you worry."*
:   *"You're not thinking of causing trouble here in this beautiful city, now are you? 'Cause I'd strongly advise against such foolishness."*
:   *"Yes? What is it?"*

When exiled:

:   *"I'll always be a commander, even if those Stormcloak dogs have stripped away my power."*
:   *"The Legion will regain control of this city. Mark my words."*

### Dampened Spirits

*"Oh come now, this is mead... not some wine to be sipped and savored."*

*"I said move!"*

**Commander Caius**: *"Well, Sabjorn. Now that you've taken care of your little pest problem, how about I get a taste of some of your mead?"*
**Sabjorn**: *"Help yourself, milord. It's my finest brew yet... I call it Honningbrew Reserve. I think you'll find it quite pleasing to your palate."*
**Commander Caius**: *"Oh come now, this is mead... not some wine to be sipped and savored."*

After pouring himself a taste of the poisoned mead, Commander Caius will start to feel bad:

**Commander Caius**: *"By the Eight?! What... what's in this?"*
**Sabjorn**: *"I... I don't know. What's wrong?"*
**Commander Caius**: *"You assured me this place was clean! I'll see... see to it that you remain in irons for the rest of your days!"*
**Sabjorn**: *"No, please! I don't understand..."*
**Commander Caius**: *"Silence, idiot! I should have known better... to trust this place after it's been riddled with filth."*
**Sabjorn**: *"I beg you... please. This is not what it seems!"*

The sickly Caius will then walk over to Mallus and say:

:   *"You... you're in charge here until I can sort this all out."*

While Mallus accepts the responsibility, he will walk over to Sabjorn again:

:   **Commander Caius**: *"And you... you're coming with me to Dragonsreach. We'll see how quickly your memory clears in the city's prisons. Now move."*
:   **Sabjorn**: *"Look, I assure you, this is all just a huge misunderstanding!"*

The captain will then draw his weapon and shout:

:   *"I said move!"*

## Notes

- Caius' dialogue after the Stormcloaks have taken Whiterun suggests that he wasn't intended to be exiled to the Blue Palace, but rather be allowed to stay in Whiterun without his rank.
  - This issue has been addressed by version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:USKP "Skyrim:USKP"). Caius' `CWExile` AI package is removed, and he instead stays in [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") for the remainder of the game.

## Bugs

- Caius may not be exiled if the Stormcloaks capture Whiterun and will still be present for the mead tasting during Dampened Spirits instead of Sinmir. **?**

# Skyrim:Commander Maro

## Overview

| Commander Maro (RefID: 0004BCC5) | | | |
