Commander Maro

**Commander Maro** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H") and the leader of the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") stationed in Skyrim, responsible for the [Emperor's](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") security on his visit. His son, [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro"), is also a Penitus Oculatus officer: you will be ordered to kill him in the quest [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security"). Commander Maro later destroys the majority of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") in retaliation for his son's death, attacking their sanctuary and killing several members in [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate"). It is possible to exact revenge on him in [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"). You can find him during this quest on the docks outside [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He will express shock and fear at the fact that you survived his purging of your Sanctuary and immediately attack you to finish the job. Alternatively, if you kill [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") during [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") and start [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!"), he will send you to the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") and have you kill everyone there. He will pay you 3,000 [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") once your task is complete.

Commander Maro wears a set of Penitus Oculatus equipment. This includes the [Penitus Oculatus armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Armor "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Armor"), a pair of [Penitus Oculatus bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Bracers "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Bracers"), and a pair of [Penitus Oculatus boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Boots "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Boots"). He is equipped with a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword").

## Related Quests

- **[To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire")**: Attempt to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") while disguised as the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet").
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

### Breaching Security

Commander Maro will have a conversation with his son Gaius Maro, regarding his safety before he leaves:

**Gaius Maro**: *"Father, you worry too much. I'll be fine."*
**Commander Maro**: *"I know you will. But all the same, remember everything I said. Stay alert, and when you get to the cities, make your observations and move on."*
**Gaius Maro**: *"I understand, But you're being paranoid. I'm inspecting security, not charging off into battle. There's not a lot that can go wrong."*
**Commander Maro**: *"Son, when the Emperor's safety is concerned, anything could go wrong. Off with you, now. And good travels."*
**Gaius Maro**: *"Farewell, father. I'll return as soon as I'm able."*

If you talk to Commander Maro when this conversation has finished, he will only say: *"Trust me, we have nothing to say to one another."*

### To Kill An Empire

During this quest, Maro will be guarding the door to the Emperor's Tower. If you engage in conversation with him, he will say:

:   *"Stop right there. The tower is off limits until further notice."*
:   **(Show Maro the [Gourmet's Writ of Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage"))**
:   *"What's this now? ...order of his eminence... ...possessor of these papers... the "Gourmet"... By [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"). The Gourmet!"*

If you are wearing [chef's](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic") [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), Maro will continue with:

:   *"I... I'm sorry! Your clothes... of course... I should have realized! Please, excuse my ignorance. Gianna, the castle chef, has been eagerly awaiting your arrival. You should proceed to the kitchens straight away."*

If you're wearing any other clothes, he will instead say:

:   *"I... I'm sorry! I didn't realize! We... we had no idea who to expect, you understand. You're not dressed as I would have suspected... But please, don't let me keep you. Proceed to the kitchens straight away. Gianna, the castle chef, has been eagerly awaiting your arrival."*

Either way, Maro will end with:

:   *"[Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna") will be overjoyed to meet you. She's in the kitchens."*

If you try to talk to him after this point, he will only say:

:   *"Just go right into the tower, then straight ahead to the kitchen. Gianna's expecting you."*

After you leave the Emperor's Tower in Solitude you will be ambushed by Commander Maro and three Penitus Oculatus Agents. Commander Maro will be clapping as you get near the ambush. He will then tell you:

:   *"That man was, by far, the most insufferable [decoy](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(decoy) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (decoy)") the Emperor has ever employed. I'm glad he's dead. Ah, but I'm even happier that you killed him. You, an assassin for the Dark Brotherhood, have just made an attempt on the Emperor's life. Would have succeeded, had it been the real man. Surprised? So was I, when a member of your "Family" came to me with the plan. We worked out a deal, you see. An exchange. I get you, and the Dark Brotherhood gets to continue its existence. But you know what? I've changed my mind. How about this? I kill you, and butcher each and every one of your miserable friends? Your Sanctuary's being put to the sword right now. That's what I think of this "deal." You killed my son! All of you! And now you'll pay the price. Kill him/her. And make sure there's nothing left to bury."*

Commander Maro and his three Penitus Oculatus Agents will then attack you. You can defeat his three agents, but you can only knock Commander Maro unconscious.

### Hail Sithis!

If you wait near him at the Solitude docks, you may overhear a conversation between him and another Penitus Oculatus agent, as seen below:

:   **Penitus Oculatus Agent**: *"And the outpost at Dragon Bridge?"*
:   **Commander Maro**: *"It'll be shuttered by the end of the month."*
:   **Penitus Oculatus Agent**: *"Very good. And you'll be returning to... Well, if you don't mind me asking, where exactly will you be going now, sir?"*
:   **Commander Maro**: *"Hmph. Now there's an excellent question. An excellent question, indeed. Truth is, as soon as the Emperor sets sail, I'm resigning my position."*
:   **Penitus Oculatus Agent**: *"Oh... I see. Well then, let me be just say that it's been an honor serving under you Commander Maro."*
:   **Commander Maro**: *"The honor has been mine. You should be proud of what we've accomplished here. The Dark Brotherhood is no more. And the Emperor, finally, is safe."*
:   **Penitus Oculatus Agent**: *"Yes sir."*

Upon seeing you at the docks, he will be very angry and will greet you by saying: *"By the gods... you! But it can't be. You're dead. You... Yeaaaahhhh!"* He will then initiate combat. Your only option now is to kill him; the guards may assist you.

### Destroy The Dark Brotherhood!

After a guard has directed you to Maro, you can inform him of Astrid's death:

:   **A guard sent me. I killed the leader of the Dark Brotherhood.**
:   *"The leader of the Dark Brotherhood? You mean Astrid? Dead? And this is no jest? Ha! This is the stroke of good fortune. Long have I watched the Dark Brotherhood's movements... waiting for the time to strike. That time is now! My agents have recently acquired the passphrase to their Sanctuary. It is, "Silence, my brother." Every assassin in that hole must be put down! You, my friend. You've slain their leader. This honor should be yours. Do this, and you will be rewarded most handsomely!"*

If you talk to him before all of the Dark Brotherhood lies dead, he will say:

:   *"We have a chance to destroy the Dark Brotherhood, forever. It's all up to you."*

When you have defeated all of the Dark Brotherhood members, you can report back to him and he will be overjoyed:

:   *"By all I hold holy... Can it be true? Have you actually done it? This is a great day, my friend. You have struck a blow against darkness that will not soon be forgotten! Here, as promised - a most generous reward."*

You will then get 3,000 gold as a reward for destroying the Dark Brotherhood. Afterwards, he will only have one greeting:

:   *"I'll make sure the Emperor himself hears of all you've accomplished. You've made Skyrim a better place."*

## Notes

- During To Kill An Empire, Maro uses the expression *"By Azura"*. This is odd, as the expression is usually associated with [Dunmer](/wiki/Lore:Dunmer "Lore:Dunmer"); indeed, Maro is the only non-Dunmer in the entire game to use it.
- Whether you attack him first or you provoke him into attacking you, no guards of any kind will ever come to help Maro. This is because he is a member of his own unique crime faction, which makes it so that other guards don't react to any crimes involving him.
- If you do not kill Maro during Hail Sithis!, he will remain standing in place by the Solitude docks for the remainder of the game. This is due to him only having a singular AI package, keeping him rooted in place and lacking any cleanup code or scripting normally seen in similar cases.

## Bugs

- Maro can potentially be chosen as the target of radiant [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") intimidation quests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19603)) He has been added to the [CR04ExclusionFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:CR04ExclusionFaction "Skyrim:CR04ExclusionFaction") in order to prevent this.

# Skyrim:Commoner

## Overview

| Commoner | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Misty Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Misty_Grove "Skyrim:Misty Grove") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0003DC4C |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |

A Commoner in [Misty Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Misty_Grove "Skyrim:Misty Grove")

**Commoners** are [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") found at [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine")'s banquet in [Misty Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Misty_Grove "Skyrim:Misty Grove"). They have no unique dialogue and spend all their time feasting.

There are four variants of each Commoner, making space for two of each variant at the table. They all carry a [tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard") and a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), although their appearance and clothes differ:

**Commoner #1** wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") with a pair of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothing") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209aa "Skyrim:Clothing").

**Commoner #2** wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing").

**Commoner #3** wears a [cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00017696 "Skyrim:Clothing"), a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing").

**Commoner #4** wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452e "Skyrim:Clothing") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452f "Skyrim:Clothing").

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

# Skyrim:Companion Ghost

## Overview

A Companion ghost in [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb")

| Companion Ghost (RefID: 000FF133) | | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [The Faction For Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Faction_For_Ghosts "Skyrim:The Faction For Ghosts") | | |

**Companion Ghosts** are ghosts of ancient [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") buried with [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor") in [his tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb").

They are equipped with full sets of [Ancient Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord "Skyrim:Ancient Nord") armor and weapons. They will often charge in with a power attack if they have a melee weapon and can detect the player at a long range.

Companion ghosts can be of various levels, thus featuring different health values and combat effectiveness, though they all share the name "Companion Ghost", making distinguishing the more dangerous ones impossible outside of combat.

## Notes

- Companion ghosts are not hostile to the [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") in the tomb, and vice versa.
- To fight the ghosts at close quarters, it is best to shield bash, get in a few hits, then move around behind them and repeat the process. As the melee ghosts often swarm you, a [staff of chain lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning") can be helpful, as it will stagger any group of enemies it strikes.
- None of the ghosts can be looted after death, as they do not leave behind any remains; they also cannot be pickpocketed. However, ghosts that use archery might leave released Ancient Nord arrows behind.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://dev.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Companion_Ghost&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. This article is about the Imperial version of this mission. For the Stormcloak version, see [Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)").

.jpg)

The broken Stormcloak Wagon

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the Rift Imperial Camp.
2. Find evidence at [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep").
3. Search [Anuriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel")'s room until you find the evidence.
4. Confront Anuriel about the evidence.
5. Report back to Rikke.
6. Attack the caravan.
7. Report to Hadvar.

### Report for Duty

At the Rift Imperial Camp, Legate Rikke will inform you that [Anuriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel"), steward to the [Jarl of Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver"), is involved with the Thieves Guild. She wants you to obtain evidence of this so that it can be used to leverage her into cooperating with the effort to regain the Rift for the Empire. She informs you that the mission will require *"stealth and discretion".* If asked, she will tell you that your destination is Riften and mark [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") on your map.

### Find the Evidence

The evidence is inside a dresser in Anuriel's room.

You may prefer to do this quest midday, while she is in the main hall rather than in her room. Although not always necessary, you may wish to take some steps to [make yourself stealthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak#Remaining_Undetected "Skyrim:Sneak") as you must evade a guard who patrols the hallway leading to Anuriel's room and then steal the item undetected. If this guard sees you, he will warn you a few times that you are trespassing and may then attack you if you remain in his presence. However, you may also avoid this guard by waiting until he walks to the other end of his beat.

If you stand in front of the Jarl facing her, you will see an open door to a hallway behind. A guard patrols the interior of this hallway. Watch for him to pass. After he walks to the left, wait a second or two, then go in and take a right. Anuriel's room is just around a corner. Steal the [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(Anuriel) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (Anuriel)") from inside the dresser, making sure that you are not observed. As an extra precaution, you may wish to close the door before you take it. Once you've taken the letter, show it to Anuriel.

### Confront Anuriel

Once you've shown Anuriel the letter, she'll lower her voice and ask you to follow her to discuss the matter privately. She informs you that if you stick closely to her, the guards won't bother you. She will lead you back into her room.

Once in the room, any conversation you have with her will result in her offering to give you information about a large shipment of gold and weapons in exchange for your silence. A successful persuasion will also cause her to offer a leveled amount of gold in advance, albeit angrily. Anuriel will tell you that the valuables are being transported by a wagon caravan in the area of Windhelm. She will relate that the wagon is heavy, and thus will be slow-moving, but is also heavily guarded.

| Levels | Reward (if Persuade succeeded) |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

### Report back to Legate Rikke

Inform Legate Rikke about the wagon. She will be pleased to learn of this, and will tell you that she has some scouts positioned in the area where the wagon is traveling. She will ask you to meet the men, overpower the rebels guarding it, and take possession of the valuables. She will mark your map with the rendezvous location, which is about halfway between Riften and Windhelm.

### Meet the Men

Upon arriving you'll find an old ally, [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar"), commanding the Imperial scout troops. He will acknowledge your past adventures and engage in some philosophizing about war and killing. You can skip this dialogue if you like. When you mention the wagon, Hadvar will inform you that he was tracking it already, and is curious how you know about its cargo. You can tell him or not. Depending on your dialogue choices, you may learn that the wagon is now stranded a short distance away, and that you are outnumbered by the rebels.

### Ambush the Rebels

Hadvar will say that he has a plan. If asked about it, he will suggest that although you are outnumbered, you can even the odds by employing the following strategy: First, he says that *"we"* will take out the Stormcloak sentry and then he and his scouts will situate themselves overlooking the camp. Then, you are to infiltrate the Stormcloak's position and create a distraction, at which time the scouts will unleash an archery attack. You can agree to this or let him know that you'll handle it on your own.

If you agree to work together with Hadvar, you can proceed immediately or tell him to wait. If it is daytime, you can suggest that you wait until nighttime, which he will think is a good idea. If you suggest waiting, you can let him know when you are ready. Once you do so, you will note in your journal that will now follow him and ambush the enemy scout.

02.jpg)

A vantage point for ambushing the sentry

Hadvar will suggest that you follow him, keep low, and hold your fire. He will walk and then stop a short distance away and may say *"We'll take care of the sentry when he makes his next round."* He may also tell you *"Fire on my word"*. Hadvar and his men will crouch in a sneaking position and face directly north with weapons drawn. From the plan he originally laid out, it may seem that you are to wait until Hadvar and his scouts take out the sentry; this will never happen. Apparently when Hadvar said "we" will take out the sentry, he meant that *you* will take out the sentry. The closest way to follow the plan is apparently to place yourself just in front of Hadvar, facing the same direction as the others. Sneaking, creep forward through the two trees in front of you. Ahead of you, the sentry pauses at the far right end of a patrol route, offering the best position for targeting with an arrow. You may need to move slightly ahead and to the left to see the place where the sentry pauses.

When the sentry is killed, your objective updates to *"Take over the caravan."* While Hadvar will repeat the idea that you are to sneak into the camp while his team positions themselves above it, things will again go not quite according to plan: quite likely, only Hadvar will position himself above the camp and attack with arrows. The other two soldiers will run directly into the camp and begin fighting. You have no chance to "infiltrate the camp," as was suggested.

Your allies will generally take care of the Stormcloaks with or without your help, and the battle should be quite easily won. After the last enemy falls, your objective will update to *"Report to Hadvar."*

If you then merely approach Hadvar, he will remark that you "make quite a team." Your work here is done, and the quest will complete at this point.

You can then loot the camp, including the chest of valuables in the back of the wagon, although this is supposed to be collected later to support the war effort.

If you will continue to pursue The Reunification of Skyrim quest, report back to Legate Rikke at the Rift Imperial Camp to obtain orders for your final mission to regain the Rift. When you approach her, she will acknowledge your performance, reward you with leveled gold, and say that she *"will send some men to collect the prize. We can use the weapons here, and I'll send the coin to Solitude."*

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- This quest and [Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") are different radiant versions of the same quest.
- If [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- You can later revisit the camp where you ambushed the rebels. The chest in the wagon will respawn and can be opened by lockpicking.
- If you have completed [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand") the guard will not challenge you.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- Hadvar occasionally will not allow you to report to him before the battle. **?**
  - Simply attacking the caravan without help will cause the quest to skip to the next stage, and Hadvar will join the fight.
- Hadvar occasionally will not allow you to report to him after the battle, which will make it impossible to finish the quest.
  - Leaving the area and waiting for a few in-game days before trying to talk to him again can allow you to finally report to him.
- This quest becomes available after completion of the previous one in the [Civil War Questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") and activates (even if it doesn't appear in your journal) upon your next load of the cell of [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (usually relocated to [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")). If you do so prior to reporting to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") (for example to get the leveled gold reward for the previous quest) the game activates this quest incorrectly causing a bug by generating and extra non-quest item copy of the [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(Anuriel) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (Anuriel)"). **?**
  - After the completion of the previous quest, avoid Rift Imperial Camp and Legate Rikke, go straight to report to General Tullius instead. Upon your next approach to Legate Rikke, this quest will have set up correctly. This skips the leveled gold reward for the previous quest.

## Quest Stages

| Compelling Tribute (CWMission07) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Legate Rikke has sent me to investigate the possibility of blackmailing Anuriel. As Laila Law-Giver's Steward, she might be able to provide important information and assets. *Objective 10:* Find evidence |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Blackmail Anuriel |
| 30 |  | Anuriel gave me information about a delivery of weapons and coin headed toward the enemy capital. I should return to camp and inform Legate Rikke. *Objective 30:* Report to Legate Rikke |
| 40 |  | Legate Rikke has sent me to meet with a scouting party that should be in the area of the enemy shipment. Together we will over power the enemy and secure the weapons and coin. *Objective 40:* Meet the men |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Follow Hadvar and ambush enemy scout |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Take over the caravan |
| 65 |  | *Objective 60:* Take over the caravan |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Report to Hadvar |
| 200 | ☑ | I have successfully blackmailed Anuriel and captured a shipment of enemy weapons and coin. |
| 205 | ☒ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 100:* Report success to Legate Rikke |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25, 41, 51, 55, 100, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWMission07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWMission07`.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find evidence.
2. Blackmail [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek").
3. Report to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
4. Meet the men.
5. Take over the caravan.
6. Report to [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof").

### Blackmail

After reporting to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), you will be told that [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek"), the steward of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), is secretly a worshipper of Talos and that you will need to find some evidence of this, and then convince him to help the Stormcloaks. Head to Markarth and go into the [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). Find Raerek's quarters, located to the right as you walk towards the throne. There is a guard there who may or may not talk to you. Don't go up the stairs; instead, take a right and look left. Guards frequently patrol the halls at all hours, however Raerek will be attending to the Jarl throughout most of the day. Sneak in the room, you need to pick the lock, so make sure you have some lockpicks with you. In the dresser against the wall, directly in sight from the doorway, you will find an inscribed amulet of Talos.

Show the amulet to Raerek and he will tell you to follow him, leading you to his quarters. When you get in his quarters he will immediately start dialogue, assuming you want to extort something from him. Asking him if you could come to some sort of agreement will have him mention a shipment of silver and weapons; selecting any topic except the "All right, it's a deal" one will give you the chance to use speech to gain a leveled amount of gold. After he tells you where the wagon is, he will take his amulet back and you will have to return to Galmar.

| Levels | Reward (if Persuade succeeded) |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

### Ambush

Return to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") at the Reach camp. After telling him that there is a shipment of coin heading to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), he will tell you to meet with some of his scouts that are situated along the road and ambush the wagon. Once you find them, speak with their leader [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof"). He will inform you that the wagon had an accident and is stranded up the road. He will then tell you that he and his men will eliminate the sentry on top of the hill and that you should go in and distract the Imperials so that the Stormcloaks can shoot them. You can also tell them to stay there while you just go in and slaughter.

If you decide to go with Ralof's plan, tell him you're ready and then creep along with him and his men until he stops at a rock. He will then command his men to fire, and they will kill the guard on the ledge and take up positions along it. Now you have to head down to the Imperials. When you approach them, they will pull out their swords and tell you to move along. Simply attack them and Ralof's men will begin shooting the Imperials. Kill all the Imperials and talk to Ralof. That will complete the quest and you will have to head back to Galmar.

### Reward

Report back to Galmar Stone-Fist at the Reach Stormcloak Camp and get a gold reward.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- If [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- The chest on the wagon is locked, but you are free to loot it.
- This quest and [Compelling Tribute (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") are different radiant versions of the same quest.

## Bugs

- You may find multiple copies of Raerek's Inscribed Amulet of Talos in the chest and Raerek will only take one back.
- You may not find an Amulet of Talos in the chest, making the quest impossible to complete. This will also make future quests with the Stormcloaks impossible to complete. To fix this bug, simply go complete other quests for a while and keep coming back to check inside of the drawer to see if the Inscribed Amulet of Talos is there. **?**
-  The horse that appears next to the broken wagon in the camp will disappear from the game world once Ralof thanks you for your help upon completion of the quest. If you are riding the horse when it disappears, the game will crash to desktop. **?**
- At the end of the ambush, Ralof doesn't respond to any conversation for some reason, freezing the quest.
  - Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout on Ralof may work to resolve this.
  - The horse in the camp may be being treated as an enemy, causing Ralof to be in a combat state. Killing the horse or making it friendly by riding it may solve this.
- If you have the [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") bounty bug, you cannot enter Markarth or complete this quest. **?**
  - You are able to still do this quest if your bounty is too high. Hopefully if you have already been to the keep, you can fast travel there. Once inside you can kill the guards at the front and then sneak around and hope you aren't found by Faleen, since she can't die. Just reload if she finds you. Once you get to the door, open it and sneak over to the dresser to find the blackmail piece and the rest works like normal. Eventually, the Stormcloaks take over and your Reach bounty disappears.
  -  Use the console command `tdetect` to turn off AI detection while talking to Raerek, otherwise wait in his room until he goes there to sleep, and confront him there.

| Compelling Tribute (CWMission07) | | |

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Blackmail Raerek |
| 30 |  | Raerek gave me information about a delivery of weapons and coin headed toward the enemy capital. I should return to camp and inform Galmar Stone-Fist. *Objective 30:* Report to Galmar Stone-Fist |
| 40 |  | Galmar Stone-Fist has sent me to meet with a scouting party that should be in the area of the enemy shipment. Together we will over power the enemy and secure the weapons and coin. *Objective 40:* Meet the men |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Follow Ralof and ambush enemy scout |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Take over the caravan |
| 65 |  | *Objective 60:* Take over the caravan |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Report to Ralof |
| 200 | ☑ | I have successfully blackmailed Raerek and captured a shipment of enemy weapons and coin. |
| 205 | ☒ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 100:* Report success to Galmar Stone-Fist |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25, 41, 51, 55, 100, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWMission07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWMission07`.

# Skyrim:Confidence (NPC)

## Overview

Confidence

**Confidence** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who is an aspect of [Pelagius the Mad's](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad") [mind](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman"). During the related quest, the much larger [Anger](/wiki/Skyrim:Anger "Skyrim:Anger") will be beating up Confidence, and you will be tasked with evening the odds with the help of the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack").

Confidence wears the common bartender [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes").

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

## Notes

- Unlike most of the other NPCs in the Mind of Madness, he can be pickpocketed, but only after Anger is defeated.

# Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell

## Overview

The location where the ritual takes place, on the roof of the Hall of Attainment

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor"), after reaching level 90 Conjuration, and receive the spell, [Summon Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Summon_Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells").
2. Go to the top of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") and cast Summon Unbound Dremora. Speak to it, then defeat it.
3. Cast Summon Unbound Dremora again and speak to it.
4. Defeat the [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora") and summon it again. Talk to it and receive the [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone").
5. Talk to [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") and receive your reward of the Master Conjuration Spell, Flame Thrall.

## Detailed Walkthrough

To start this quest, go to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") when you have level 90 in [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"). Talk to [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") and ask him if you can learn more about [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"). He will need a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone"). He will give you the spell [Summon Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Summon_Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells"). Head to the top of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Note that you need to go outside. Stand in the circle and use the spell. This will summon an Unbound Dremora.
Summoning the Unbound Dremora will initiate a conversation:

*"You dare bring me here? You will be punished."*.

At this point, two dialogue options will appear:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| ***"You will do as I say!"*** | ***"I summoned you. I control you now."*** |
| *"I serve no mortal!"* | *"You control nothing, mortal!"* |

The Unbound Dremora in combat

At this point it will engage in combat and you must kill him. After he is dead you must summon him in the circle again, and he will speak again:

*"I am not your plaything, worm!"*

At this point another two dialogue options will appear:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| ***"Are you ready to submit?"*** | ***"Admit that I control you."*** |
| *"Never!"* | *"I'll tear your heart out first!"* |

At this time he will become hostile and you must kill him. Summon him again and speak to him:

*"I am not yours to toy with!"*

From here you can reply with:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| ***"Will you submit, or do I need to banish you again?"*** | ***"I can do this all day."*** |
| *"I...I submit. What is your bidding, master."* | *"No, I... I submit. No more."* *"What is your bidding?"* |

Both of these options will lead to you saying:

***"Bring me a Sigil Stone. Now."***

He will then say:

*"Yes, my lord/mistress. Summon me again, and I shall have your stone."*

At this point in the quest, he will banish himself and you must summon the Unbound Dremora once more. When you do it will say:

*"Your Sigil Stone. Lord Dagon is... less than pleased at its loss."*

The Sigil Stone will be added to your inventory and the Quest Objective, Deliver the stone to Phinis, is assigned. Bring the [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") to [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") and he will give you [Flame Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Flame_Thrall "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells"). You will also, now have the option to buy the Master level Conjuration Spells; [Frost Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Frost_Thrall "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells"), [Storm Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Storm_Thrall "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells"), and [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells#Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells").

## Notes

- The [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") you are rewarded in this quest is used to unlock the full potential of the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge"). Daedric Atronach Forge recipes, both with and without the Sigil Stone, will begin to show up in random loot after you receive the objective to "Report to Savos Aren" during [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), regardless of this quest.
- The final Unbound Dremora will remain until it is killed and can move outside of the circle in response to any threats or danger.
- If you have the [Disarming Bash](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarming_Bash "Skyrim:Disarming Bash") perk, you can disarm the Unbound Dremora and then pick up his weapon.
- If you cancel the dialogue and sneak behind it, it is possible to pickpocket its weapon with a high enough skill. It carries a random enchanted main weapon and an iron dagger. You may also attack it from behind to weaken it before talking to it and resuming dialogue. But if you kill it without resuming dialogue, you will not be able to summon it again.
- It is possible to defeat the Unbound Dremora and pick up his weapon before he has been banished.
- It is possible to get two Sigil Stones. Once the Sigil Stone has been received from the Unbound Dremora, it can be placed in the Atronach Forge. You can then go to Phinis Gestor and 'give' him the stone, when you talk to him again and ask "What did you see?" he will thank you and give you the second Sigil Stone and Flame Thrall.

## Bugs

- The Unbound Dremora summoning sequence may result in freezes or may not complete.
  - If it gets stuck, reloading and trying again should fix it.
- The Dremora will automatically attack Delphine, Esbern, and most animals such as Barbas or any pets you have with you. This will make the quest impossible to complete, as the Dremora will not open dialogue and these characters cannot be killed.
  - Taking them to another zone and telling them to stop following you, will allow you to continue.
  - If you need to keep your follower, then summon something else far enough away (maybe a Dremora Lord if you purchased the spell) and tell your follower to attack it. While they are fighting, run to the summoning spot. The quest should proceed normally.
- The Dremora may not leave after having given you the Sigil at the last summoning. He will instead stand there in a state where he cannot be damaged nor interacted with. If you have finished the quest, however, this will not impact the ability to summon Dremora Lords or use the other Master spells. The ritual candles are never cleaned up either, despite Phinis Gestor making a big deal of safety.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The Unbound Dremora may be hostile towards [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") members as well as [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas"), if they happened to be there when the spell is cast.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.
- Once the Sigil Stone is delivered to Phinis Gestor, the Flame Thrall spell may not be given.
  - If this occurs, loading the last save or autosave and trying again should fix the issue.
- Defeating the Unbound Dremora while it is paralyzed can cause it to die and leave a lootable corpse rather than simply be banished. This breaks the quest and requires you to reload a save to complete it.
- Disintegrating the Unbound Dremora will leave a lootable ash pile rather than banishing it. This also breaks the quest and you will need to reload. **?**
- You might not be able to talk to Phinis if [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") quest is active.
  - Completing that quest should fix the problem.
- After receiving the Sigil Stone and taking it to Phinis Gestor, he will not acknowledge it. He will go through the first two lines of dialogue then begin to walk around.
  - The quest starter dialogue option should still be available, going through the full dialogue again fixes the problem.
  - Reverse pick pocketing the sigil stone should allow him to recognize it in his inventory.
- If the Unbound Dremora is summoned during a dragon attack, the Dremora will run away.
- If you make your Conjuration skill Legendary before casting Summon Unbound Dremora, the Dremora won't speak with you.

  **Mod Notes**: The entire quest is contingent on the player's Conjuration skill; when the skill drops below 90, the quest becomes inactive and the OnSpellCast event that updates the DremoraFlag variable stops firing.

  - Raising your Conjuration skill to 90 or above once again will allow the quest to proceed normally.
- If you attempt to give Phinis the stone after waking him up he will acknowledge the stone and therefore the quest cannot be completed.
  - Reloading the save and waiting until he is outside of the Hall of Countenance will fix this issue.

## Quest Stages

| Conjuration Ritual Spell (MGRitual03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Phinis Gestor has told me that in order to inscribe powerful Conjuration spells, he'll need a sigil stone from an Oblivion gate. To get one, I'll need to summon an Unbound Dremora and bend it to my will. *Objective 10:* Summon and subdue an Unbound Dremora |
| 70 |  | Phinis Gestor requires a sigil stone to inscribe powerful Conjuration spells for me. I subdued an Unbound Dremora and had it retrieve one for me, which I should now take to Phinis. *Objective 20:* Deliver the stone to Phinis |
| 200 | ☑ | I have subdued an Unbound Dremora and had him retrieve a sigil stone for me, which Phinis Gestor has used to inscribe the Master Conjuration spells. In exchange for doing this, he has given me the first of the spells. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 30, 40, 50, 60.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRitual03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRitual03`.

# Skyrim:Conjurer

## Overview

**Conjurers**  are [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") specialists who prefer to summon [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") in combat. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). These mages belong to the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of conjurer you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level conjurers even at high levels, but boss-level conjurers will always be at the highest possible level.

### Conjurers

A Novice Conjurer blasting a gout of fire with a ward ready in his other hand

Conjurers use Destruction magic and summon allies to fight for them in combat, and they carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, conjurers have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, conjurers have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers have the same gear as lower-level conjurers, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

[^1](#note_SecretPyromancer)This Master Conjurer appears in leveled lists with conjurers, but is actually a [Pyromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Pyromancer "Skyrim:Pyromancer"), and has the appropriate class, spells, and perks for a generic [fire mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") of the same level.

### Conjurer Bosses

An Apprentice Conjurer and her Flame Atronach

Apprentice Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level conjurers listed above. Conjurer Adept, Conjurer, Ascendant Conjurer and Master Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers listed above, with the exception that Conjurer Adepts and Conjurers have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"), or [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning, Fireballs, or Ice Storms.

## Related Quests

### World Interactions

- **[Warlock fighting off bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Warlock_fighting_off_bandits "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Bugs

- Most conjurers will summon their atronachs before attacking you with Destruction magic, but conjurers with the Conjure Storm Atronach spell will not summon Storm Atronachs. This is likely due to an issue with their combat style script.

# Skyrim:Conjurer

## Overview

**Conjurers**  are [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") specialists who prefer to summon [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") in combat. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). These mages belong to the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of conjurer you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level conjurers even at high levels, but boss-level conjurers will always be at the highest possible level.

### Conjurers

A Novice Conjurer blasting a gout of fire with a ward ready in his other hand

Conjurers use Destruction magic and summon allies to fight for them in combat, and they carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, conjurers have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, conjurers have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers have the same gear as lower-level conjurers, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Conjurer Bosses

An Apprentice Conjurer and her Flame Atronach

Apprentice Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level conjurers listed above. Conjurer Adept, Conjurer, Ascendant Conjurer and Master Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers listed above, with the exception that Conjurer Adepts and Conjurers have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"), or [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning, Fireballs, or Ice Storms.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Warlock fighting off bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Warlock_fighting_off_bandits "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Bugs

- Most conjurers will summon their atronachs before attacking you with Destruction magic, but conjurers with the Conjure Storm Atronach spell will not summon Storm Atronachs. This is likely due to an issue with their combat style script.

# Skyrim:Conjurer

## Overview

**Conjurers**  are [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") specialists who prefer to summon [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") in combat. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). These mages belong to the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of conjurer you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level conjurers even at high levels, but boss-level conjurers will always be at the highest possible level.

### Conjurers

A Novice Conjurer blasting a gout of fire with a ward ready in his other hand

Conjurers use Destruction magic and summon allies to fight for them in combat, and they carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, conjurers have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, conjurers have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers have the same gear as lower-level conjurers, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Conjurer Bosses

An Apprentice Conjurer and her Flame Atronach

Apprentice Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level conjurers listed above. Conjurer Adept, Conjurer, Ascendant Conjurer and Master Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers listed above, with the exception that Conjurer Adepts and Conjurers have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"), or [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning, Fireballs, or Ice Storms.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Warlock fighting off bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Warlock_fighting_off_bandits "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Bugs

- Most conjurers will summon their atronachs before attacking you with Destruction magic, but conjurers with the Conjure Storm Atronach spell will not summon Storm Atronachs. This is likely due to an issue with their combat style script.

# Skyrim:Conjurer

## Overview

**Conjurers**  are [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") specialists who prefer to summon [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") in combat. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). These mages belong to the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of conjurer you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level conjurers even at high levels, but boss-level conjurers will always be at the highest possible level.

### Conjurers

A Novice Conjurer blasting a gout of fire with a ward ready in his other hand

Conjurers use Destruction magic and summon allies to fight for them in combat, and they carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, conjurers have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, conjurers have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers have the same gear as lower-level conjurers, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

[^1](#note_SecretPyromancer)This Master Conjurer appears in leveled lists with conjurers, but is actually a [Pyromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Pyromancer "Skyrim:Pyromancer"), and has the appropriate class, spells, and perks for a generic [fire mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") of the same level.

### Conjurer Bosses

An Apprentice Conjurer and her Flame Atronach

Apprentice Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level conjurers listed above. Conjurer Adept, Conjurer, Ascendant Conjurer and Master Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers listed above, with the exception that Conjurer Adepts and Conjurers have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"), or [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning, Fireballs, or Ice Storms.

| [Gauldur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur "Skyrim:Gauldur") | [Reachwater Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwater_Rock "Skyrim:Reachwater Rock") | The shade of a great wizard who drew his power from a legendary [amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gauldur_Amulet "Skyrim:The Gauldur Amulet") |
| [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne") ([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) | [Ruunvald Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Temple "Skyrim:Ruunvald Temple") | An Altmer woman who charmed [Moric Sidrey](/wiki/Skyrim:Moric_Sidrey "Skyrim:Moric Sidrey") and some [Vigilants of Stendarr|](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant") |
| [Paratus Decimius](/wiki/Skyrim:Paratus_Decimius "Skyrim:Paratus Decimius") | [Mzulft Aedrome](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft_Aedrome "Skyrim:Mzulft Aedrome") | A [Synod](/wiki/Skyrim:Synod "Skyrim:Synod") mage working in the ruins of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Warlock fighting off bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Warlock_fighting_off_bandits "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Bugs

- Most conjurers will summon their atronachs before attacking you with Destruction magic, but conjurers with the Conjure Storm Atronach spell will not summon Storm Atronachs. This is likely due to an issue with their combat style script.
