# Skyrim:Conjurer

## Overview

**Conjurers**  are [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") specialists who prefer to summon [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") in combat. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). These mages belong to the [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of conjurer you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level conjurers even at high levels, but boss-level conjurers will always be at the highest possible level.

### Conjurers

A Novice Conjurer blasting a gout of fire with a ward ready in his other hand

Conjurers use Destruction magic and summon allies to fight for them in combat, and they carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, conjurers have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, conjurers have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers have the same gear as lower-level conjurers, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning"), [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs"), or a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Conjurer Bosses

An Apprentice Conjurer and her Flame Atronach

Apprentice Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level conjurers listed above. Conjurer Adept, Conjurer, Ascendant Conjurer and Master Conjurer bosses have the same inventory as the Master Conjurers and Arch Conjurers listed above, with the exception that Conjurer Adepts and Conjurers have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"), or [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning, Fireballs, or Ice Storms.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Warlock fighting off bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Warlock_fighting_off_bandits "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Bugs

- Most conjurers will summon their atronachs before attacking you with Destruction magic, but conjurers with the Conjure Storm Atronach spell will not summon Storm Atronachs. This is likely due to an issue with their combat style script.

# Skyrim:Constance Michel

## Overview

| Constance Michel (RefID: 00019DE5) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | | |
| Location | [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019DE5 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013350 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 30 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 60 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleYoungEager](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleYoungEager "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleYoungEager") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [Riften Honorhall Orphanage Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Honorhall_Orphanage_Faction "Skyrim:Riften Honorhall Orphanage Faction"); [TownRiftenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction "Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction") | | |

Constance Michel at the Riften Orphanage

**Constance Michel** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who works at [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). While the orphanage leader [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") mistreats the children with beatings and verbal abuse, Constance is entirely different and takes great pride in making the children feel safe and loved.

With Grelod shouting at her and the orphans all the time, Constance's workday is a long one. She sleeps behind closed doors near the dining area until 5am and immediately starts wandering around the orphanage, at times cooking or relaxing on one of the available chairs. At 10am she enters the food storage room and stays there for an hour before she proceeds with her wandering. At 3pm, it is time for the children's only meal of the day and Constance will reluctantly take a seat next to Grelod and listen to her complaints for an hour. She spends her evening strolling around as usual until her late bedtime at 1am. There are two exceptions to this routine; when you enter the orphanage for the first time, she will stand in the background while Grelod yells at the orphans. If Grelod is killed, however, she will run around in wild panic, screaming and yelling, while the mistreated children will cheer with joy. Constance will remain in this state until you complete the quest Innocence Lost, at which point she will resume her normal schedule.

Her only possessions are her clothes: a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). Her room contains the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Purloined Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Purloined_Shadows "Skyrim:Purloined Shadows")*.

## Related Quests

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

### Innocence Lost

If spoken to directly:

:   **Tell me about Grelod the Kind.**
:   *"I will do nothing of the sort. You have no business here. I'm sorry, but you really must leave."*

If she witnesses Grelod being killed:

:   *"Grelod... murdered. Here. I... I need... air... You... you... Get out of here! Get out!"*
:   *"Just... leave here! Leave us alone!"*

## Dialogue

Constance and [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind")

When approached, it becomes clear that she is terrified that your presence will anger Grelod and she will say:

:   *"You really shouldn't be in here."*
:   *"I'm sorry, but the children aren't up for adoption right now. You should go."*
:   *"My only concern is for the children. The poor darlings have no one else."*

After witnessing Grelod's introductory speech to the orphans:

:   **Is Grelod always like that?**
:   *"Sadly, yes. Even the townsfolk have taken to calling her 'Grelod the Kind.' Her very existence has become something of a running joke. Grelod runs this orphanage because she's old, and set in her ways, and doesn't know any other life. These children need love, and comfort. I try... But... I'm sorry, you should go. The children aren't up for adoption, and it's cruel to get their hopes up. Besides, Grelod hates... visitors."*

When exiting conversation she will encourage you to leave with:

:   *"If there's nothing else, I really must ask you to leave."*

When all is said and done and the [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") quest is completed, Constance will be the only adult in the orphanage and as such, the new leader. The children will be much happier, although Constance will never forget what happened:

:   *"I can't believe Grelod is dead. I had no love for the woman, but to be murdered, in cold blood..."*

### Adoption

After [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, Constance will start talking about adoption:

:   *"This war has created so many orphans, and so few are willing to open their hearts to them..."*

Speaking to her:

:   **Could I adopt one of your children?**

Her response will differ depending on a few conditions:

| Condition | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") not completed | *"I'm sorry, no. Grelod is the headmistress here, and she's decided not to allow any adoptions right now. I... I wish things were otherwise. All of these children deserve a better home. But there's nothing I can do."* |
| Innocence Lost completed | *"Why yes, yes of course! What a wonderful surprise!"* |
| Adoption process has been started before | *"Very well, let's try this again..."* |
| You have already adopted two children | *"You already have children, don't you? I'm sorry, but I can't let you adopt anyone else."* |

When you can adopt she will ask you questions:

:   **What do I need to do?**
:   *"First, I'll need to ask you a few questions.
    Your name?"*
:   **<Player Name>.**
:   *"What do you do for a living?"*

Depending on your progress in the game, you may have a variety of responses to choose from:

| Dialogue Option | Reply |
| --- | --- |
| "I'm the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin")." | *"What? If you aren't going to be... wait. [Shor](/wiki/Lore:Shor "Lore:Shor"), you're serious! Well, I... all right then."* |
| "I'm the Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions")." |
| "I'm the Archmage *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")." |
| "I'm an [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")." | *"What? What kind of a joke is this? Look, don't waste my time. Come back when you're ready to discuss this for real."* |
| "I'm a [Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")." |
| "I'm an Adventurer." | *"Mmm-hmm."* |
| "I'm a Mercenary." |

:   *"Where will your child be living?"*

If you don't own a house with a children's bedroom:

:   **I... hadn't thought of that.**
:   *"...Look, let's be realistic. You're an adventurer. It's not exactly a safe or reliable profession.
    I need to be sure your child will have a safe, stable home to grow up in.
    Show me that you can support a child. Buy a house. Furnish it. Then come back, and we'll talk."*

Speaking to her again:

:   *"I'm sorry, but until you own a home with a room for your children, I can't allow you to adopt anyone."*

If you speak to her again after buying and furnishing a house:

:   **I've purchased a home and furnished it. Can I adopt a child now?**
:   *"Yes, of course! That's wonderful news!"*

If you do own a house with a children's bedroom:

:   **At my house in <City>.**

If you own a [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") house, you'll be able to move your child there.

:   **At <House Name>.**

Once you have successfully completed the questionnaire, she will say:

:   *"That's all I need from you. Congratulations! I think you'll make an excellent parent.
    Go meet the children and decide who you'd like to adopt.
    Once you've made a decision, I'll collect their things and be sure they make it over to your house."*

Speaking to her again:

:   *"Go on, speak to the children! I'm sure they're eager to meet you."*

If you return to her after adopting one of the orphans, and this is the first child you've adopted, she will say:

:   *"Congratulations! If you ever want to adopt another child, you'll always be welcome here."*

Or if you have now adopted two children:

:   *"Congratulations. I hope you have a wonderful life together."*

## Conversations

Observing daily life in the orphanage will reveal the cause of Constance's nervousness. When she least expects it, Grelod may yell *"Constance!"* and share a random complaint about one of the children. A tired Constance will then say *"Yes, Grelod?"* and choose from at set of overbearing replies to calm her down:

**Grelod**:

:   *"[Samuel](/wiki/Skyrim:Samuel "Skyrim:Samuel") is getting to be a problem. Fancies himself something of a 'leader' to the other children. Put an end to the nonsense, or I will."*
:   *"[Hroar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroar "Skyrim:Hroar")'s crying is keeping me up at night. I'll give you one chance to talk the tears out of him, or he's getting the belt."*
:   *"I can't abide Samuel's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *constant talk of his parents. 'They're coming for me.' 'This is only temporary.' The boy must accept his fate."*
:   *"Seven septims are missing from my purse. I know it was [Runa](/wiki/Skyrim:Runa_Fair-Shield "Skyrim:Runa Fair-Shield"). You get those coins back, or by [Stendarr](/wiki/Lore:Stendarr "Lore:Stendarr"), I'll see her rot in the dungeon."*
:   *"This place is filthy. I've a mind to cancel all town privileges unless those brats start pulling their weight."*
:   *"The stores are running low. We'll need to water down the milk again. Besides, don't want the little darlings getting fat."*
:   *"We haven't had an adoption in months. At this rate, we'll be stuck with these brats forever. We need to get the word out. A sale, if need be."*

**Constance**:

:   *"All right. I'll take care of it."*
:   *"I'll handle it. No need to blow things out of proportion."*
:   *"Please, just let me handle it. It's not a problem."*
:   *"Okay, okay. I'll deal with it."*

## Notes

- Constance's love for the orphans has not gone unnoticed, as the children will describe the differences between Grelod and Constance's way of handling things. Hroar will tell you, *"I ain't afraid of the old hag. Still, I wish Constance was in charge. She treats us real good. Constance, sometimes she gives me little snacks. Which is good, 'cause we only get but one meal. Late, too, in the afternoon. I'm a growing boy. I need as much food as I can get."* Runa Fair-Shield will, when asked about Grelod, add: *"I hate her. Everyone hates her. She's the meanest person I ever met. Sometimes she even locks us in the... room. Constance tries to stop her, and is real good to us, but it's never enough."* Constance's kindness will eventually save her life, as escaped orphan [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") specifically requests that she be spared, saying, *"Please don't kill Constance Michel. She really is kind."* Sure enough, killing Constance will cause all the children at Honorhall to hate you.

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen") | | → Next | [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") | | |

Magic anomalies created by the Eye's power surge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren").
2. Defeat the [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") attacking [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").
3. Report to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine").

## Detailed Walkthrough

College members mourning the death of the Arch-Mage

### Tragedy at the College

As you regain consciousness after witnessing part of the battle between [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") and the Arch-Mage [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"), Mirabelle Ervine will be standing above you, telling you to get on your feet. Gather your wits and find her visibly shaken and upset. Tell her you feel okay, and she will tell you that Ancano is doing something with the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus") and that the Arch-Mage is missing. This will begin the quest. Head to the College's central courtyard where you will find the Arch-Mage's body and a group of mages. [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") will approach you and inform you that whatever killed the Arch-Mage has also affected the town of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). He asks you to go there and save the town.

### No Time for Grief

Cross the bridge, where [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") and [Arniel](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") will be waiting. Faralda will inquire about the situation. Explain that Winterhold is in imminent danger and proceed to the town. Faralda and Arniel will follow and assist you in the battle that awaits. You will find the town has become infested with a swarm of [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly")—fast moving balls of energy whose attacks deliver [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") damage. They explode upon defeat, leaving behind [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in their "ghostly remains". Faralda and Arniel prove valuable allies in this battle and, with their help, you defeat the ten anomalies and secure the town. Arniel will remain in the town while you return to the College to report back to Mirabelle.

### The Staff of Magnus

When you find Mirabelle, she will tell you that she and Tolfdir are trying to keep the Eye contained, but are in dire need of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus"). When you tell her that you must venture to [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") for the staff, she softens a bit from her concern and grief. She intimates that Savos Aren had just recently given her a mysterious [torc](/wiki/Skyrim:Torc_of_Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Torc of Labyrinthian"), cryptically telling her that she would know what to do with it when the time came, and she believes it was meant for you. She also gives you [Savos Aren's amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren%27s_Amulet "Skyrim:Savos Aren's Amulet") to aid you on your journey, believing that you will be better served by it. The [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") quest begins here.

## Notes

- An unused NPC known as the "[Dremora Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs "Skyrim:Unused NPCs")", internally referred to under the Editor ID of `MG05Messenger`, was once intended to play a role in this quest, although what exactly this role entailed, is unknown.
- If your horse is stabled within the city, the anomalies can quickly surround it and kill it. Simply rush down there at the start of the quest, hop on your horse, ride it out of town, hop off, and then sprint back on foot and join the fray, unless you have [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere"), then he can probably stay with you in the fight.
- At higher levels, the anomalies can be used to train [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") very effectively, due to their large numbers and low attack power.
- The souls of magic anomalies are leveled.
- All College NPCs will either disappear or lose all dialogue options until the next quest is finished, which temporarily prevents you from advancing certain quests or using College services. Any NPCs who have been made followers or [stewards](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") will also lose their dialogue options until the quest is complete.
- You cannot loot the Arch-Mage's body.
- If you leave a follower somewhere away from the college or the town of Winterhold, when you go to speak with Mirabelle they may be there.
- Enthir travels to Winterhold on Tirdas and Turdas at 10pm and stays there until midnight, even while this quest is active. This means that if the battle takes place during this timeframe, he may join in on the fighting and be a useful ally as an [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") character.
- Even after finishing the quest and talking to Mirabelle, magic anomalies will appear in the town of Winterhold and attack the guards.
- It is advisable to finish sub-quests involving the townsfolk before triggering the anomalies, as they are known to kill NPCs in town.

## Bugs

- [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") can be found wandering between Windhelm and Winterhold after being exiled if this quest was running at the time. This is due to the quest giving him an AI package that makes him return to his editor location, this being Winterhold, even when in exile.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13139))
- You may not get the initiating quest once the Arch-Mage is dead, and there will not be a group of mages surrounding him. This problem may be solved by loading a save several quest stages before the Eye of Magnus explodes.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `startquest MG05` will start the quest if talking to Savos Aren does not update the previous quest and Mirabelle does not give the quest.
  -  To get the quest to start, complete all Winterhold related quests that you have active including any under miscellaneous quests.
- One of the anomalies may not appear and is likely under the world or in a wall, and you may find that it has fallen to the bottom of the cliff near the city.
  - Fast traveling back to the town may fix this.
  - Also, entering another cell such as the inn can cause it to move out of the wall.
- You may not receive the quest after the Eye of Magnus has been overloaded.
- If a dragon appears while you are fighting the anomalies, the dead dragon will not give you a dragon soul, and when you kill the anomalies, the quest will mark as being moved on the next stage but you won't be able to enter the College, and people won't talk to you. It is recommended that you reload to a save from before the dragon appeared. **?**
- After killing the anomalies, the entrance to the Hall of the Elements may be inactive.
  - Wait for an NPC to enter and fix the door for you; saving and reloading won't fix this.
  - It may also be possible to reset the door yourself by clicking around or near the edges of the door.
- If you go into the Arch-Mage's quarters before going outside, you may encounter him alive but without any dialogue when you try to speak to him.

## Quest Stages

| Containment (MG05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Assess the damage to the Great Hall |
| 20 |  | Ancano has done something to the Eye of Magnus, causing the orb to release incredible amounts of energy, and possibly putting the area in danger. I need to find the Arch-Mage and make sure he's safe. *Objective 20:* Find the Arch-Mage |
| 30 |  | Ancano has done something to the Eye of Magnus, causing the orb to release incredible amounts of energy, damaging the College and killing the Arch-Mage. The town of Winterhold may be affected as well, and needs to be secured. *Objective 30:* Protect the town of Winterhold |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Defeat the creatures infesting Winterhold (<Global=MG05CreaturesKilled>/10) |
| 50 |  | Winterhold now appears to be safe from the creatures attacking it. Mirabelle needs to be informed of what's going on. *Objective 50:* Report to Mirabelle Ervine |
| 200 | ☑ | The town of Winterhold has been secured for now, but the Eye of Magnus cannot be reached and continues to jeopardize the College. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 25.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG05`.

# Skyrim:Convince Nikulas to stay in Skaal Village

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Dreamshadow](/wiki/User:Dreamshadow "User:Dreamshadow"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Daric Gaersmith](/wiki/User:Daric_Gaersmith "User:Daric Gaersmith"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Counsel a [young Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") on the dangers of life as an adventurer.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") |
| Location(s): | [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") |
| Reward: | 5 [Ashen Grass Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod"), 5 [Emperor Parasol Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Parasol_Moss "Skyrim:Emperor Parasol Moss"), 5 [Scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla")) |
| ID: | DLC2SkaalVillageFreeform2 |

The mother and her son

*"I know it must be hard for an adventurer such as you to understand this, but we Skaal live very boring lives."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") about her son.
2. Convince [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") to stay in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
3. Return to Edla.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Return to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") after the quest [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal") and you can find [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") wandering around the village. She may tell you *"My son's heart is restless. He wants to see the world beyond our lands, and nothing I say will change his mind."* If you ask her about her son, she will provide you with more detailed information. His name is [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)"), and he is a good lad, a strong and loyal young man. However, Edla wishes her son wasn't so eager to leave the village. If you are willing to talk to him, she will be quite happy. *"You would do that? I know he would listen to you. You've been out there in the wide world. You know its perils."* She hopes you can convince him.

You can find Nikulas sitting on a bench outside [their house](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla%27s_House "Skyrim:Edla's House"). You may talk to him about his mother and his dream. He will admit *"That's right. I want to go out into the world and earn great glory. I want to hunt the deadliest creatures and claim vast riches."* He is weary of the life in Skaal Village and he wants to do something with his life other than farm, fish, and hunt deer. You may choose various ways to convince him to stay at home or remind him to think about his mother before making the final decision.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I do understand. In fact, I'm willing to help you get started.  - Take this. Just give your mother some more time. **(Bribe)** | You are? I admit, I was not expecting to hear that.  - **Passed**: Yes, you're right. She still mourns for my father, and having me near brings her comfort. You have my oath that I will not leave the village until my mother is ready to let me go. - **Failed**: I am grateful for your offer, outsider, but I am Skaal. All that I need, I was born with. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Edla **Failed**: Nothing |
| The world is dangerous, and you're not ready for it. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Well, I know there is some danger, of course, but I didn't think it would be that bad. If the risk is truly so great, I will train with [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood") and hone my skills. Perhaps in three or four winters, I will truly be ready. **Failed**: There is no fear in my heart. My father's blood flows in my veins, and he was a mighty warrior. I will face any danger. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Edla **Failed**: Nothing |
| You'd abandon your mother when she needs you most? **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: There is truth in your words. She has not been herself since my father's death. **Failed**: I know that it would be difficult for her, at least for a time, but I am a man now. I have the right to choose what life I will. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Edla **Failed**: Nothing |

At last, he will see that in his eagerness for adventure, he has forgotten his duties as a son and as a Skaal. He will thank you for your wisdom.

Return to Edla and tell her that Nikulas has agreed to stay. *"May the All-Maker bless you with many sons and daughters, outsider. Once again you have shown that you are a true friend of the Skaal."* She will reward you with some herbs that are unique to the land, including five [Ashen Grass Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod"), five [Emperor Parasol Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Parasol_Moss "Skyrim:Emperor Parasol Moss"), and five [Scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw"). She still thinks the reward can hardly be equal to the joy in her heart.

## Bugs

- Nikulas may not receive the quest-relevant dialogue options. Disabling and re-enabling him via the console resolves this issue. **?**
- Finishing this quest may not raise Edla's disposition towards you.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2SkaalVillageFreeform2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2SkaalVillageFreeform2`.

A corpse

This **corpse** of a male [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") soldier, with a full set of [Imperial Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"), is likely a guard to the members of the team from [The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition"). Finding the corpse does not update the quest. It is located in [Nchuand-Zel Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel_Quarters "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel Quarters"), near the torture room on the left.

Corpse of a female Imperial soldier

This **corpse** of a female [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") soldier is near the entrance of [Nchuand-Zel Armory](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel_Armory "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel Armory") in the camp made with a bedroll and a small barrel. She wears a full set of [Imperial Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"), and was likely a guard to the members of the team from [The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition"). Finding the corpse does not update the quest.

Corpse of a male Imperial soldier

This **corpse** belongs to a male [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") soldier and can be found near the corpse of the female soldier, at the entrance to [Nchuand-Zel Armory](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel_Armory "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel Armory").

| Corpse (RefID: 0003A40C) | | | |

It is located in the second room of [Forelhost Stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost_Stronghold "Skyrim:Forelhost Stronghold"), on the left of the fire.

# Skyrim:Corpselight Farm

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Farm: Corpselight Farm ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Corpselight+Farm)) | | |

| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Corpselight Farm, Falkreath

**Corpselight Farm** is a small farmstead located in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

Corpselight Farm interior

It is run by [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") and his wife, [Indara Caerellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Indara_Caerellia "Skyrim:Indara Caerellia"). Their daughter was recently killed when a passing farmhand named [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") went berserk and ripped her to shreds with his bare hands. When first visiting Falkreath her parents can be found at the burial service being held in the graveyard beyond the rear of their plot. It consists of only one interior zone, *[Corpselight Farm](#Corpselight_Farm)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Indara Caerellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Indara_Caerellia "Skyrim:Indara Caerellia")  [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

### Exterior

There is a small farm plot behind it with the plants and livestock listed below. There is a cart filled with six cabbages and a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") at the rear of the house, as part of the farm plot.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 12 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  5 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  12 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 1 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") | 1 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Corpselight Farm

This is a single-room home, with a cupboard holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right, in the southern corner and along the southwest wall are several barrels of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). Opposite the cupboard on the northwest wall is a long wooden table and bench. On the table are two bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and various pieces of cheese. Hanging above from the ceiling are four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear").

Opposite the door in the middle of the northwest wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a bowl of [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") on the mantelpiece. By the hearth is a pile of firewood and [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). To the right of the fireplace is a cupboard holding two common books, a copy of *[The Apprentice's Assistant](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Apprentice%27s_Assistant "Skyrim:The Apprentice's Assistant")* and a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")*. Above the cupboard are two more bunches of frost mirriam and three more bunches of elves ear.

Coming out from the northeast wall is a large double bed with end tables either side holding a bottle of wine and one of alto wine. Next to the bed on the southeast wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, with a round wooden table and two chairs to the right of the chest. On the table are a bottle of each; wine and alto wine and a loaf of bread. Right next to the entrance is a basket containing three more chicken's eggs.

## Notes

- The grain mill can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.
- The Prima guide mentions the name of the farm comes from a past resident that helped develop the idea of "cultivating" the witchlights and wisps that illuminate the edges of the town graveyard.
- Corpselight Farm also appears in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Corpselight_Farm "Legends:Corpselight Farm").

Corpulus Vinius

**Corpulus Vinius** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [food vendor](/wiki/Skyrim:Food_Vendor "Skyrim:Food Vendor") and the owner of [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He will rent out a room to you for 10 gold a night and offers merchant services. He is the father of [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") and [Minette Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Minette_Vinius "Skyrim:Minette Vinius"), who both want to take over the inn when Corpulus retires. Until then, they help out with the daily maintenance. Corpulus also has a cousin in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), the proprietor of the [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern"), [Faida](/wiki/Skyrim:Faida "Skyrim:Faida"). Should anything happen to Corpulus, Sorex will take over running the inn.

Corpulus can be found welcoming guests and offering his services in the taproom of the Winking Skeever 24 hours a day, without ever pausing to eat or sleep. He will only leave his spot behind the counter if you rent a room for the night, and politely show you to your room.

Corpulus wears a set of barkeep [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:Key to Winking Skeever") to the tavern, a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When greeting you:

:   *"Welcome to the Winking Skeever, friend."*
:   *"If you need a good rumor or two, I think I can oblige..."*
:   *"Traitors, civil wars, dragons. Bah. Those troubles don't cross my doorway. So sit, relax."*
:   *"Welcome to the Winking Skeever. Take a load off and enjoy the atmosphere."*
:   **Why is this place called the Winking Skeever?**

    :   *"Well, as it turns out, I had a pet [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") when I was a boy and he used to wink."*
    :   **You kept a skeever as a pet?**

        :   *"They were smaller back then."*
    :   **I guess that's as good a reason as any.**

        :   *"I thought so."*
:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"Magic? You're on the wrong side of Skyrim. You want Winterhold... that College there. They teach it.
    Otherwise you can try the [Jarl's wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor"). I wouldn't, though."*

When asked about rumors, he will point you towards a few local quests, starting with [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"):

:   *"I've heard [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") is hanging around the Wells District, looking for new blood to hire."*

Next, he will point you towards the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"):

:   *"I think the Bards College might be looking for recruits. You should speak to the head of the college, [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo"), if you're interested."*

He also mentions a traveler from Dragon Bridge:

:   *"Varnius Junius stopped by here on his way to court. He was worried about something. I'm sure [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") could tell you what."*

Lastly, he heard rumors about a [crazy person](/wiki/Skyrim:Dervenin "Skyrim:Dervenin") wandering the streets near the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"):

:   *"People say there's a man wandering the streets near the Blue Palace. He seems distressed but he's not making any sense."*

When you exit conversation he will say one of the following:

:   *"Remember the Winking Skeever next time you're footsore."*
:   *"Need anything, you just say the word."*

## Conversations

*"That's it! I'm not retiring, ever! End of discussion!"*

While the family business runs smoothly on the surface, there are times when Sorex Vinius seems too keen on running the tavern, although he will not talk about it when his father is listening. This becomes even more evident if you witness another random conversation between Corpulus and Sorex, where little Minette also shows interest in running the inn, at times causing Corpulus to raise his voice:

:   **Corpulus:** *"It's been a good week, my boy! Loud customers mean good cheer, and good cheer means a full till! You know, I ought to retire and leave you to run the Skeever, son!"*
:   **Sorex:** *"I don't know, father... There's a whole world out there I want to see."* / *"You'd just spend your time here, bossing me around and yelling for more drinks. You're practically retired already..."*
:   **Minette:** *"I could run the Skeever! You even said I'm almost as smart as you!"* / *"Why not let me run the Skeever? I already know lots about it!"*
:   **Corpulus:** *"Don't be a silly girl! Running a bar's no job for a young lady."* / *"Hah! A girl running a bar? Don't be ridiculous, Minette!"*
:   **Minette:** *"What about 'Auntie Faida' in Dragon Bridge? She runs a bar, and you said she's one of your favorite girls!"* / *"But you always say you want more girls in the bar to begin with!"*
:   **Sorex:** *"Oh, brother..."* / *"Hah!"*
:   **Corpulus:** *"That's it! I'm not retiring, ever! End of discussion!"* / *"Well, you see, that's a little complicated, and... you know what? Never mind. Guess I'm not retiring anytime soon."*

The following conversation can only happen between 5pm and 9pm:

:   **Corpulus:** *"Bring up some more mead, my boy. This cask's nearly tapped!"*
:   **Sorex:** *"Yes, father. Which cask should we open?"*
:   **Corpulus:** *"Just bring any of them, lad! Can't risk thirsty customers without mead to drink, even for a second!"* / *"Any of them! Just hurry up! No time for a debate when customers are thirsty!"*
:   **Minette:** *"Bring the Blackbriar*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *195 Berry-Blend. It should be at its peak right now, and if it doesn't get served soon, it'll only go bad."* / *"We just got a cask of Old Gold 200 that has a crack in it. Better serve it now before it goes bad."* / *"Fat Toad 190 is always a crowd-pleaser. Father could probably charge extra."*
:   **Sorex:** *"Good idea, sis. Maybe you ought to be in charge!"*
:   **Corpulus:** *"Yes, yes, fine. Just hurry! Mustn't keep the customers thirsty!"*

## Bugs

- Corpulus (or his replacement if he's dead) can occasionally be seen sitting on the bar stools in front of the bar due to the radius of his main Solitude innkeeper package being overly large.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17284)) While the issue has been reportedly corrected, some players have reported the problem persisting even then.

Corrupt Agent

The **Corrupt Agent** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who may appear in [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost") in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") during the quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). He will only be enabled if the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") picks him as the contract giver.

He will be chosen randomly from a list of ten people who performed the Black Sacrament and want someone killed. When approached, he will choose between a total of ten possible targets, hand you a leveled amount of gold and blindly expect you to carry out the task.

The Corrupt Agent wears a set of [Penitus Oculatus armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Armor "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Armor") with a matching [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Helmet "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Helmet"), pair of [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Bracers "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Bracers"), and pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Boots "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Boots"). He wields an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and carries a copy of *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")*.

He shares his dialogue with the nine other potential quest givers; see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever#Detailed_Walkthrough "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") for details.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

# Skyrim:Corsair

## Overview

**Corsairs** are hostile NPCs unique to the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload"), a pirate ship docked near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). They are under the command of the elusive Captain Volf, who is never encountered in-game.

| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |

| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | Any Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Very Aggressive |

One of two corsairs sitting at a table

This **Corsair** is found on the Dainty Sload, sitting at a table in a kitchen-like room in the downstairs portion of the ship, with a separate corsair.

The corsair patrolling the decks

These two **Corsairs** are male [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") on the Dainty Sload. They each carry a [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar") and a small amount of gold. They wear [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots"), and [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers"). One sits at a table in the downstairs kitchen-like room with the corsair in the section above. The other is at the top, guarding the entrance to the interior of the ship.

Cosnach

**Cosnach** is a drunken [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who is usually found at the bar in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"). He is a porter for the [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company"), which can be found directly across the path from the Silver-Blood Inn. Cosnach thinks himself a good worker, but his employer, [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet"), complains about his constant drinking and says the only reason she doesn't fire him is because his cousin [Imedhnain](/wiki/Skyrim:Imedhnain "Skyrim:Imedhnain") is her assistant. He claims that the reason he spends all his time drinking is the multiple [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") raids on supply caravans, hurting business.

Cosnach gets up at 8am, and proceeds straight to the Silver-Blood Inn, where he spends the next 16 hours drinking. At midnight he will finally stop drinking and walk to his bed in [the Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") to sleep; before repeating his schedule the following day.

You can offer him an alcoholic beverage for which he will be grateful. If you either offer him an alcoholic beverage or accept his offer of a brawl and win, he will become an available [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). With that he becomes a potential [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") partner, and can be recruited into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"). You may also recruit him as a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") if the [Hearthfire DLC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.

Cosnach wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") and a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Cosnach%27s_Room "Skyrim:Key to Cosnach's Room") to his room as well as a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

### Fight! Fight!

If you talk to him about his mentioned bet:

:   **You say something about a bet?**
:   *"I'm drunk, and it's been a while since I had a good fight. A hundred septims says I can take ya, bare-handed."*

:   :   **I've got better things to do.**
    :   *"Milk drinker."*

:   :   **You're on. (Brawl - 100 gold)**
    :   *"That's the spirit! Let's go."*

Should you accept his bet without 100 gold in your possession:

:   *"Hey, I may have had a few, but I can still count. You don't have a hundred septims on you."*

When you have defeated him in hand-to-hand, he will get up and say:

:   *"Wait, I can still fight. No, no I can't."*

When he hands you the prize, he will dryly state:

:   *"Fair fight. Here you are."*

He is now available as a follower and is a potential candidate for marriage.

### The Forsworn Conspiracy

If you ask him about [Margret](/wiki/Skyrim:Margret "Skyrim:Margret") while he is in the Silver-Blood Inn during [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy"):

:   **Does a woman named Margret stay here?** (If she is alive)
:   *"Oh yeah. Pretty little thing. Been sitting by the fire all day."*

:   **Did a woman named Margret stay here?** (If she is dead)
:   *"Oh yeah. Pretty little thing. Had a room here I think. Ask the innkeeper."*

## Dialogue

When approached he can say:

:   *""Check the shipments" Lisbet says. "There are no shipments" I says."*
:   *"There's no shipments coming in, so I do nothing. Just drink."*
:   *"No breaks for a good worker out here."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **So where do you work?**
:   *"Arnleif and Sons Trading Company. I'm a porter. Just some muscle hired to move heavy packages. But we don't get any shipments in. Forsworn attack every caravan. So all I do is sit here and drink."*

When greeting you, he might ask:

:   *"You a fighting man/girl? How about a little bet?"*

He can exit conversations with:

:   *"I think I'm going to get another drink."*
:   *"Bye."*

## Conversations

Cosnach may be seen having conversations with his fellow drunk [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") or the innkeeper [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr"):

Degaine and Cosnach

**Degaine**: *"Give us a coin, Cosnach. You'll just spend it on cheap ale, anyway."*
**Cosnach**: *"Like you won't do different?"*
**Degaine**: *"I'm a cripple. I have a reason to be drinking."*
**Cosnach**: *"And I'm a porter with no shipments coming in. You're not getting any coin from me, Degaine."*

**Cosnach**: *"How did you manage to cripple yourself, Degaine?"*
**Degaine**: *"Mining accident, back when I was in prison for being a pickpocket."*
**Cosnach**: *"You're lying. You're not quick enough to be a pickpocket. What's the real reason?"*
**Degaine**: *"Fell off the top of the cliff after a drunken party with the priestesses of Dibella."*
**Cosnach**: *"I don't buy that story, either."*
**Degaine**: *"Too bad. That one's my favorite."*

**Kleppr**: *"Another drink, Cosnach? A porter with Arnleif and Sons deserves nothing but the finest here."*
**Cosnach**: *"All your drinks are watered down, Kleppr. You aren't fooling me, and you know Lisbet can't afford to pay me enough for the finest drinks anyhow."*
**Kleppr**: *"I wasn't aware that Lisbet was having trouble, Cosnach. Is Arnleif and Sons not doing a good turn of business these days?"*
**Cosnach**: *"What are you, blind? That store is empty. Forsworn get almost every shipment that comes in."*
**Kleppr**: *"That's just terrible. I'm so sorry to hear that."*
**Cosnach**: *"No you aren't."*

## Unused Dialogue

Cosnach has unused dialogue tied to a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") he was once meant to give you. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

### FreeformMarkarthB

:   **Something wrong with the shipments from Arnleif and Sons?**
:   *"What shipments? Never get anything in. Forsworn just take everything. Well, maybe not everything. Heh heh heh."*

:   **What do you mean "maybe not everything?"** (Possibly based on disposition)
:   *"What? Oh, nothing. Nothing."*

:   **(Favor) What do you mean "maybe not everything?"**
:   *"Maybe when a shipment does come in, some items go "missing." Maybe I sell a few things here and there to my friends at a lower cost. What do you say?"*

:   **(Favor) What do you mean "maybe not everything?"**
:   *"Not now. Talk to me when I'm not in the store. Don't want Lisbet to hear."* (If spoken to at Arnleif and Sons, where he normally can never be found)

:   **Found any "missing" items I could buy?**
:   *"Anyone catches you with this, I've never seen you before."*
:   **Found any "missing" items I could buy?**
:   *"Not here. Lisbet might see."* (If spoken to at the store)

## Unused Scenes

Cosnach was also meant to have conversations with his boss, Lisbet, but as they are meant to play inside Arnleif and Sons, and he never sets foot there, they can't play:

:   **Cosnach**: *"No shipments have come in."*
:   **Lisbet**: *"What do I pay you for, to stand around all day? You're supposed to be bringing goods to the store."*
:   **Cosnach**: *"There are no goods to bring to the store. That's what I'm saying."*
:   **Lisbet**: *"Lazy oaf."*

:   **Lisbet**: *"Where are my goods? Did the shipment come in?"*
:   **Cosnach**: *"Only a few things came today. [Cedran](/wiki/Skyrim:Cedran "Skyrim:Cedran") said he'd drop it off later."*
:   **Lisbet**: *"Cedran said he'd... what am I paying you for? Next time, you bring the shipment in yourself."*

## Notes

- Although his default gear is light armor, Cosnach is actually more proficient in heavy armor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. His class was changed to [CombatBarbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatBarbarian "Skyrim:CombatBarbarian").
- As is the case with all members of the `FavorJobsDrunksFaction` faction, the option to give Cosnach an alcoholic drink never goes away. Even if he is an active follower, you can give him a drink any time during your travels. The drink(s) can be taken from his inventory later if desired.

## Bugs

- Cosnach will still have the "So where do you work?" dialogue option even if he is married and living with you, and obviously no longer working for Lisbet.

A Dark Elf courier

A Wood Elf courier

An Imperial courier

A dead courier

**Couriers** are generic NPCs who travel to deliver messages. They can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Courier_Delivering_an_Important_Message "Skyrim:World Interactions"), and will appear to hand you letters related to certain quests. A courier can appear anywhere in the province of Skyrim, as well as on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

The randomly encountered courier can either be an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial"), [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"), or [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf"). The Wood Elf is clad in a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1da "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"), and carries a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") that can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality, a random [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") of low value, a [courier's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Courier's Letter") that you can pickpocket, and an assortment of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). The Imperial carries the same items as the Wood Elf, but wears a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000330bc "Skyrim:Hat") as well as different [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"). Likewise, the Nord courier has the same inventory as the Wood Elf, except for an additional random book and wears a different [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000209aa "Skyrim:Hat"), [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Buy Dwarven artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact")**: Bring your newly-obtained [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") artifact to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.
- **[Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance")**: A friend has died. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Scare my Enemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Scare_my_Enemy "Skyrim:Scare my Enemy")**: Assault a target. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Shout - learn about word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall")**: Explore a location and learn a [Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Assist [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") in his search for the relics of [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)") in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").
- **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")**: Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

## Dialogue

They can be found walking along a road. Any attempts at conversation will only have them tell you, *"Important deliveries to make! No time for chatting!"*

During the quest [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"), you are to locate a different courier from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), albeit already dead when you arrive. He was a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") and wore a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and carried [Keening](/wiki/Skyrim:Keening "Skyrim:Keening").

The courier that delivers letters to you is a Nord wearing random farm clothes, boots, as well as a hat. Unlike the other couriers, he carries nothing else with him. He will only appear as part of certain quests, tasked to ensure important messages are in your hands. Using a [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") in public view can increase the probability of a contact with him; after doing so, he will usually appear some time later with a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_a_Friend "Skyrim:Letter from a Friend") that activates a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall"). He will also occasionally bring other kinds of messages, as detailed below.

He will approach you and say, *"I've been looking for you. Got something I'm supposed to deliver - your hands only."* He will mumble, *"Let's see here..."* before saying one or more of the following lines, depending on what he has for you:

- *"Yeah, got this note."* ([Mysterious Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)"))

:   :   "From who?"
    :   *"Don't know. Creepy fella, black robe. Couldn't see his face. Paid me a pretty sum to get that into your hands, though."*

- *"I have a letter here from [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He said it was urgent."* ([Letter from Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Letter from Quintus Navale"))
- *"I've got a letter and a lot of gold. Something about it being your [inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance")? Oh, and... sorry for your loss."* ([Letter of Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Inheritance "Skyrim:Letter of Inheritance"))
- *"A letter... not sure who from. He wouldn't say. Just that he was a friend of yours."* (Letter from a Friend)
- *"I have a letter here for you."* ([Letter from](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from "Skyrim:Letter from"))
- *"A note from someone named [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo"), in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")."* ([Letter from Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcelmo"))
- *"It's from... [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")? You've got friends in high places."* ([Letter from Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Letter from Falk Firebeard"))
- *"There's a new museum opening up in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [The owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius") is asking me to hand out invitations to travelers."* ([Museum Pamphlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Museum_Pamphlet "Skyrim:Museum Pamphlet"))

As soon as [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, he will randomly appear to give you additional letters:

- *"Here's a letter from the Jarl's steward. Looks like official business."* ([Breezehome Furnishings](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome_Furnishings "Skyrim:Breezehome Furnishings") or [Letter from Steward (Steward name) of (hold name)](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Steward_(Steward_name)_of_(hold_name) "Skyrim:Letter from Steward (Steward name) of (hold name)"))
- *"There's a [new lady](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel") in charge of the [Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). She asked me to hand out these notices to everyone I met."* ([Consider Adoption](/wiki/Skyrim:Consider_Adoption "Skyrim:Consider Adoption"))
- *"Ah, a letter from the Jarl! Moving up in the world, eh?"* ([Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name)_of_(Jarl%27s_City) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name) of (Jarl's City)") or [Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name)](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Jarl_(Jarl%27s_Name) "Skyrim:Letter from Jarl (Jarl's Name)"))

With the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on, he will arrive to give you messages from [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys"):

- *"Got this from a pretty excited looking dark elf around [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). He said it was important I got it to you as soon as I could."* ([Letter from Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys"))
- *"Another note from your friend Ralis. I hope everything is all right."* ([Letter from Ralis Sedarys 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_2 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 2"))
- *"Another letter from Ralis. He's starting to scare me a little."* ([Letter from Ralis Sedarys 3](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_3 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 3"))
- *"I've got another letter from Ralis, but this is the last thing I'm delivering for him. That place is just too much for me."* ([Letter from Ralis Sedarys 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Ralis_Sedarys_4 "Skyrim:Letter from Ralis Sedarys 4"))

Once he is done, he will say, *"Looks like that's it. Got to go."* and walk away from you. If you talk to him again, he will only say, *"Nope, sorry. Nothing."*

## Notes

- You can read the note while looking at the random encounter courier's inventory via pickpocketing, therefore avoiding any risk of being caught. Reading the courier's letter will add the named location to your map, if you haven't already found it. The courier sent to give you your mail actually doesn't hold the letter(s) in his inventory, which can be seen when paralyzing him (through spell or applied poison) and searching his inventory by crouching as he is getting back up.
- While attacking random encounter couriers found along the roads will net you a bounty for assault, you can freely attack the courier that approaches you in villages and cities without reprisal from various NPCs and guards. In addition, if you have made any friends in that particular location (such as [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci") in Whiterun, or [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") in Riften) and/or are a Thane of that particular hold, the NPCs and guards will actually attack the courier once he turns hostile. Since this particular courier is essential, he can be used for skill grinding by using magic and weaponry on him.
- If you are still on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") while doing Unearthed, the courier will approach you there, in Raven Rock. This is the only time he will not be on mainland Skyrim.
- Version 1.3.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") has courier deliveries now identify what they are delivering to you instead of an "Items added" message.
  - Version 1.1.2 of the [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch") does the same for Hearthfire deliveries.
- The courier that delivers your mail is actually the same courier each time, even though he will appear with a different set of clothes each instance that you encounter him.
- The courier appears in villages (like [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone")), cities (such as Whiterun), farms, sawmills, mines (those not occupied by anyone anything hostile), any of the private properties you might own (Creation Club houses and those added by Hearthfire), but he doesn't appear at military camps or forts taken over during the Civil War.
- You cannot hide from the mail-delivering courier, as he will initiate conversation even if you are fully hidden and were never spotted.

## Bugs

- The courier occasionally arrives wearing little or no clothes, which he never replaces. Each subsequent meeting with him will either see him wearing the same or even less clothing.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  - This can sometimes be fixed by reverse-pickpocketing new armor or clothes onto him.
- Couriers sent to deliver something to you don't handle crimes committed against them due to no crime faction being assigned to them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. The alias in WICourier has been given the script which assigns crime factions based on where the courier is being sent.
