# Skyrim:Court Wizard

## Overview

Calcelmo, author and Court Wizard in Markarth

**Court Wizards** are the [jarls'](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") personal mages who research and study magic. They can usually be found in the jarl's [palace or longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles"). They sell a variety of [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") from all of the schools of magic, and other items that are of use to mages, including [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls"). Their selection of available spells and magical items are bested only by the mages at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

In court politics they are the equals of [housecarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), except on magical matters, but less important than [stewards](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"). They are usually left alone by their jarl due to the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord")' suspicion and distrust of all things magical. They are also the only members of court that do not have to relocate if their [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") changes sides in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War").

## Court Wizards of Skyrim

The following people are court wizards:

| Hold | Capital | Wizard | Location |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **[Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch")** | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") | [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") |
| **[Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")** | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") | [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") |
| **[The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale")** | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Madena](/wiki/Skyrim:Madena "Skyrim:Madena") | [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall") |
| **[The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach")** | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") | [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") |
| **[The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")** | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah") | [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") |
| **[Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold")** | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") | [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") |

## Notes

- The jarls of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") do not employ court wizards. The absence of a wizard in Winterhold is likely due to the close proximity of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") (and the locals' disdain for magic), but the reasoning for the other two is unclear.
- [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar"), [Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran"), and [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") all belong to the court wizard faction. They are all intended as replacements for the incumbent court wizards, but Calcelmo and Wuunferth are essential, preventing Aicantar and Dravynea from being needed. Melaran is supposed to replace Sybille in the event of her death, and he will confirm this in conversation, but he will never adopt her routine or sell anything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. Melaran will replace Stentor as intended.

## Bugs

- Despite being mages, some court wizards and some replacements don't know any spells at all.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Farm: Cowflop Farmhouse ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cowflop+Farmhouse)) | | |

| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Cowflop Farmhouse

**Cowflop Farmhouse** is a small farmhouse located in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). It is home to [Ennis](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennis "Skyrim:Ennis") and [Reldith](/wiki/Skyrim:Reldith "Skyrim:Reldith"), who are both [farmers](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)"). It is at the eastern end of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"), along the road that passes through the village. It is next door to [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn"). It contains only one zone, *[Cowflop Farmhouse](#Cowflop_Farmhouse)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ennis](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennis "Skyrim:Ennis")  [Reldith](/wiki/Skyrim:Reldith "Skyrim:Reldith") |

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There are wooden steps leading up to the entrance from the road. There are two [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") found beside the building. It has a large, picturesque pasture to the east and consists of a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling"), twelve bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a chicken coop containing two nests, two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken"), fifteen [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and eighteen [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. During the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), they will also own a beloved [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") named [Gleda](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleda_the_Goat "Skyrim:Gleda the Goat").

### Cowflop Farmhouse

The front door is novice-locked the majority of the time. It is a typical farm building consisting of a simple one-room home, that is fully stocked. The house may look modest, but it does have some worthwhile loot hidden away.

Upon entering there is a cupboard on the left against the southwest wall holding various pieces of cheese, a cabbage, five [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), five [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of True Shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"). In the western corner is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and a basket containing three cabbages. Next to these along the northwest wall is a long wooden table. On the table is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two [apple pies](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and two [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). To the right of the table is an unlocked respawning wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items, and hanging from the ceiling above are two garlic braids, a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear").

Against the northeast wall is another long wooden table and bench. It holds several pieces of cheese, two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Hanging from racks above are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), four [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). In the middle of the northeast wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") in front, and by the hearth is a pile of firewood and [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). To the right of the fireplace is a cupboard holding more bottles of wine and alto wine, with more bunches of elves ear and frost mirriam hanging from the ceiling above.

Coming out from the middle of the southeast wall is a large double bed with an end table at either side. On these is a couple of bottles of wine and a filled [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). To the right, against the southwest wall is an unlocked non-respawning chest containing leveled items and small round wooden table with two chairs. On this table is a loaf of bread, a bottle of alto wine, and a bottle of wine.

## Notes

- The grain mill can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from wheat if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.
- All cupboards and end tables in the location are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

# Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shack.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shack.png) | Shack: Crabber's Shanty ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Crabber%27s+Shanty)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Fisherman](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman "Skyrim:Fisherman") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| CrabbersShantyExterior | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") (see [bugs)](#Bugs) | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") | 1 |

Exterior of the shack

**Crabber's Shanty** is a small run-down [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") on the [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal").

The shack is home to a lone [fisherman](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman "Skyrim:Fisherman"). It contains only one zone, which is the exterior zone *[Crabber's Shanty](#Crabber.27s_Shanty)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Fisherman](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman "Skyrim:Fisherman") |

### Exterior

Inside the shanty

There are two doorways into the shanty and several holes in the roof and a large glassless window in the wall, making it barely better than sleeping outside. One doorway faces east and the other faces west. There are several sacks and a barrel containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around the shanty; one small sack outside the south side of the shanty isn't marked as owned and therefore can be emptied freely. Outside the doorway to the east on a small piece of decking is an open crate containing two dead [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") that can be harvested freely. The fisherman seems to spend all of his time sitting on the edge of the decking. There is also a [bucket](/wiki/Skyrim:Bucket "Skyrim:Bucket") and an unsearchable barrel near the fisherman. There is a [clam](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") in the stream near the shanty that can be harvested for [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"), while several mudcrabs are found up and down the stream from here.

### Crabber's Shanty

Inside the shanty, there is a single owned bed in the southeastern corner. Against the west wall is a small unit holding another dead mudcrab that can be freely harvested. To the right of this is a basket containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Against the north wall is a set of shelves holding three [tankards](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard"), bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and six [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"). The tankards and bottles of ale can be freely taken, but the vegetables are owned.

## Notes

- The barrels in the house are [respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning"); however, the sacks are non-respawning and safe to store items in.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the small sack, tankards, and bottles of ale as owned like everything else.
- The [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") Creation adds a [fishing rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod"), a pair of [fishing boots](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Fishing_Boots&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Fishing Boots (page does not exist)"), and a book.
- Version 4.3.3 marks everything added with the Fishing Creation as owned like everything else.

## Bugs

- [Fast traveling](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Travel "Skyrim:Fast Travel") to this location can sometimes cause the player to spawn high in the air, only to fall to their death.
- Crabber's Shanty is erroneously marked as being in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. It has been set to be part of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") instead.

# Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Cracked Tusk Keep

**Cracked Tusk Keep** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Hunter "Skyrim:Orc Hunter") led by [Ghunzul](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghunzul "Skyrim:Ghunzul"). It contains two zones: *[Cracked Tusk Keep](#Cracked_Tusk_Keep)* and *[Cracked Tusk Vaults](#Cracked_Tusk_Vaults)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The grounds have the typical wooden palisade surrounding the keep. The guards are Orc bandits and they make good use of the many elevated positions around the keep. The western tower ruin contains a semi-buried master-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The easiest way to access the chest is to climb up the rubble from outside of the wall. An apprentice-locked chest is located on the very top of the keep, between the two rear towers. Using the keep's series of ramps and lookout platforms, approach from the west and climb/jump up the rubble to the top.
The keep's courtyard has several outbuildings designed for sustaining an army. From left to right around the courtyard is a smokehouse with a variety of [meats](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") being cured and various animal [pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelt "Skyrim:Pelt"), a small rest area containing a copy of *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*, and then the main door to the keep. Across from the door is the fully equipped smithy, complete with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). There is a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword")[*verification needed — best material?*] on top of the workbench. Inside the smithy's shed is a table with a selection of poor quality [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") and [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Light Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Light Armor Forging")*.

There are three entrances into the keep. The first, and most direct, is the front door. The second, ideal for stealth-based characters, is a level-locked door directly south of the smithy and down a flight of stairs. This is the door to the cellar and can grant an advantage against the guards in the main room. The third is a trapdoor on top of the southeast tower, which leads directly to the boss.

### Cracked Tusk Keep

Entering through the main door leads you right into the well-lit guards' area on two levels with at least two bandits; one on each level. A dresser just inside the entrance on the left has a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on top. Opposite the entrance is a cupboard holding two common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There is a counter against the northeast wall with a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot") on top. Hanging above from racks is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the right is a barrel with a basket containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and some [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). To the left of the counter is a wooden door with stairs leading down to the cellar and *[Cracked Tusk Vaults](#Cracked_Tusk_Vaults)*. There are six unowned bedrolls on the floor.

There are stairs against the rear wall leading up to the upper level, where a long table and benches are laid out with a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [leg of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast"), a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). There is a chair by the top of the stairs with an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") leaning against it. There is an end table along with several food sacks around the walls and a set of shelves against the southwest wall holding a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), five common books including a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* and several food sacks. In the eastern corner there has been a cave-in.

There is a wooden door to the southeast to the bandit leader's quarters. Through the door is a room with a fireplace on the right and a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") on the hearth that you cannot interact with. There are food sacks on either side and a ladder to the left that leads to a trapdoor exit out onto one of the towers. Opposite this is an opening to Ghunzul's bedroom, where you will find him. There is an unowned double bed coming out from the northeast wall with a dresser on the right with a copy of the [Cracked Tusk Vault key](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Vault_Key "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Vault Key") on top and a basket beside it containing two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). To the left of the bed is a set of shelves holding a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), a small coin purse, a leveled potion of healing, and nine common books. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked boss chest and in the corner a round table and chair with a copy of *The Code of Malacath* on top. Ghunzul also carries a copy of the Cracked Tusk Vault key.

Through the door on the ground floor to the northwest is a passage that descends a flight of stairs. At the bottom is a cupboard holding only clutter, with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") to the left. On your right is the room where you would arrive if entering through the leveled entrance south of the smithy. Beside the entrance is a long wooden table with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") built in. On the table is a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") and [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), while hanging above are two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and three bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right is a cupboard holding several [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), two empty random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a random potion of healing and a food sack. Beside the cupboard is an end table with a basket of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top. Opposite the table is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and a potion of minor stamina on top. There are a couple of barrels and sacks around the room and in the southwestern corner is a passage blocked by spears with an expert-locked cage on the wall, containing a button that activates the spears. The cage can be unlocked with the key taken from Ghunzul or [lockpicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") without it. Beyond the spears is a flight of stairs down to a wooden door leading to *Cracked Tusk Vaults*.

### Cracked Tusk Vaults

There are no enemies within the vaults, but the vaults have suffered quite a bit of damage from cave-ins and there are still several traps that are armed and can cause damage to the unwary. There is a passage behind the door leading down to the southeast. In front of you is a counter with a random potion of healing and two empty random soul gems on top. Beside this is a basket containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). There are a number of food sacks and barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") throughout the vaults. At the bottom of the stairs is a room with spears blocking access. To the right is a button that lowers the spears. The room contains a dresser, cupboard and set of shelves holding a small coin purse, a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Lore:Lost_Legends "Lore:Lost Legends")*, a potion of minor healing and a random poison. There is also a broken table in the corner with a potion of minor stamina, a random potion, an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and a filled random soul gem among the remains. Slightly farther along the passage, on the left is another room, again with the spears and button. Inside this room is a set of shelves holding clutter with a [fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Fox Pelt") on top and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") leaning against it, a wooden bench with a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[Rislav The Righteous](/wiki/Skyrim:Rislav_The_Righteous "Skyrim:Rislav The Righteous")* at one end and a random potion of healing at the other. There is an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on top of a couple of barrels and beside these a cupboard holding a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), a random helmet and gauntlets. Farther along the passage opens up in front of double sets of spears blocking the passage both horizontally and vertically. On the left is an unlocked chest and an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") with a set of shelves that have been knocked over by a cave-in, knocking a random potion of magicka onto some more barrels. There are pillars with levers either side of the passage that activate the spears and giving access ahead and beyond these are three [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") in a row along the central passage. These trigger [dart traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") that are easily avoided. To the left is a fourth tripwire that triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap. To the right is an adept-locked chest. At the end of the passage is a plinth with the [shards of Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shards_of_Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Shards of Mehrunes' Razor") sitting on a [weight-sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") that also triggers a dart trap. Standing to the left when taking them and jumping back allows you to avoid damage.

## Notes

- According to a [Development Map](/wiki/File:SR-map-Development_Map_02.png "File:SR-map-Development Map 02.png"), this location was originally called **Gularz Khazgur**. Its presence on the map might also imply that Gularz Khazgur was the first [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") to be implemented in the game.
  - While the overall location was called Gularz Khazgur, it seems that the keep also still existed, which would've been called **Gularz Khazgur Keep**. A [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Key_to_Gularz_Khazgur_Keep "Skyrim:Keys") to this location still exists in the files, but is unobtainable and not linked to any doors.
  - The script for [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past") still refers to this location as "Gularz", and there is also a marker present called `GularzKhazgurCenterMarkerREF` that can still be seen in the Creation Kit.
  - The stronghold of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") might have gotten part of its name from Gularz Khazgur.
  - In the final game, Cracked Tusk Keep still has various Orcish themes. It is inhabited exclusively by Orc hunters and bandits, multiple copies of *The Code of Malacath* can be found, and much of the architecture outside the fort resembles that which you would expect to find in an Orc stronghold, albeit without a longhouse. It's unknown if this layout was repurposed from the original vision of the stronghold, or if the designers added Orcish elements to the keep in reference to its former appearance.
  - Ghunzul's ancestor, as mentioned in *[The Keepers of the Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Keepers_of_the_Razor "Skyrim:The Keepers of the Razor")*, was named "Othmash gro-Gularz". It's also stated he had served time in the Imperial Legion. Stronghold Orcs who leave to serve in the Legion often take up their stronghold name during this time (as stated by [Ghorbash the Iron Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorbash_the_Iron_Hand "Skyrim:Ghorbash the Iron Hand"), who went by "Ghorbash gro-Dushnikh" during his service). This might have also been the case for Othmash, such that his last name relates to when the fort was known as Gularz Khazgur.
- The Orcs here will always be hostile, regardless of whether you are [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin"). In addition, killing the Orcs here won't cause Orcs in other locations to become hostile, as they don't belong to the same faction.
- There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") 150 feet due north of the keep.

## Bugs

- One of the Orcs here is using a generic bandit name, which is inconsistent with the others at this location.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If the quest [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") directs you here, check to see if you have already visited this location. This location does not respawn, so if you have been here before, the Moon Amulet cannot spawn here and you cannot complete the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, addresses this issue. The location will be forced to reset and anything stored here will be lost.
  - Without the Unofficial Patch, you will need to reload a previous save to get a different location from [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- The map marker location data for Cracked Tusk Keep points to a random XMarker rather than to the map marker itself.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.3, fixes this bug.
- Everything outside the dungeon may respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone". **?**

## Maps

- 

  Cracked Tusk Keep
- 

  Cracked Tusk Vaults

# Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower

## Overview

Cradle Stone Tower

**Cradle Stone Tower** is a small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") west of [Bard's Leap Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard%27s_Leap_Summit "Skyrim:Bard's Leap Summit") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

After scaling the Forsworn-filled hills at [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt") and crossing the waterfall at Bard's Leap Summit, follow the trail up the west hill, looting a chest along your way to this remote tower. An alternate and more adventurous route to the tower is by [climbing](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") the rocky formation from the unmarked crevice where [Frofnir Trollsbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Frofnir_Trollsbane "Skyrim:Frofnir Trollsbane") is located [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-105567&y=-31508.2&zoom=17&legacy=true). By doing so, you can bypass the Forsworn-infested redoubt entirely.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The tower has a total of four floors to it. The lowest level is accessed via a novice-locked gate. Inside at the top of the stairs is a broken stone table with a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") (see [notes](#Notes)) on top and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") beside it. The stairs lead down to a caved-in section with an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). There is no access from this level to the second floor. Outside of the tower is a wooden ramp that leads up to the second floor where you will encounter the only occupant of the tower, a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). The second floor also contains a sideboard opposite the doorway, holding a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis")* with a set of shelves to the left holding a random [magicka potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a flight of wooden stairs leading up to the third floor.

At the top of the stairs there is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that fires [lightning bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") that is situated across the broken floorboards to the north. There is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") to the left and a broken sideboard holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") to the right of the trap. Against the west wall is another flight of wooden stairs leading to the top floor; to the left of this is a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") sticking out of the rubble. The top floor is the smallest floor and only has a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") on it. It does offer a nice view as well.

## Notes

- A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is located right outside the entrance to the tower.
- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is located a short distance southwest.
- The random dagger and helmet don't appear to respawn.

## Bugs

- If you have already cleared Lost Valley Redoubt and fast travel to Cradle Stone Tower, the fast travel may instead place you at the word wall section of Lost Valley Redoubt. This bug will correct itself after you have cleared Cradle Stone Tower.
- The [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis")* may not be present. See the bug on the book page itself for more information.

## Overview

| Southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") East-southeast of [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade") | |

Cradlecrush Rock

**Cradlecrush Rock** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Huge cheese

The camp is near the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") downstream from [Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers") and [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade"). To reach it, follow the road east from Valtheim Towers. Shortly after a hairpin bend to the right at the bottom of the hill, you will see a ford on your left with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") visible on the other side. Follow this path up to reach the camp.

A single [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") occupies the camp, which consists of a central campfire that has been extinguished, two [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"), a stacked woodpile with a dead painted [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") on top which can be looted for [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"), an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a leveled healing potion and a leveled stamina potion next to it, and a huge pile of straw that probably serves as the giant's bed, though you will never see him sleep in it. Among the ashes of the fire are three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [sliced Eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), and an unusually large [Eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), the largest of these in the game. A single stake with a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") is cooking over the fire. A few feet west of the campfire, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a leveled enchanted helm, and a ring can be found on three separate skeletons that appear to have been crushed by a huge rock.

## Notes

- 320 feet east-northeast of the camp is an [unmarked location](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") containing a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"), an unlocked chest, and a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")*.
- Cradlecrush Rock [appears](/wiki/Online:Cradlecrush "Online:Cradlecrush") as a [fort](/wiki/Online:Forts "Online:Forts") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").
